{ASāh, 1}
evaṃ mayā śrutam | [ASāh, 1 1.1]
ekasmin samaye bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati sma gṛdhrakūṭe parvate mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena sārdhamardhatrayodaśabhirbhikṣuśataiḥ sarvairarhadbhiḥ kṣīṇāsravairniḥkleśairvaśībhūtaiḥ suvimuktacittaiḥ suvimuktaprajñair ājñair ājāneyair mahānāgaiḥ kṛtakṛtyaiḥ kṛtakaraṇīyairapahṛtabhārairanuprāptasvakārthaiḥ parikṣīṇabhavasaṃyojanaiḥ samyagājñāsuvimuktacittaiḥ sarvacetovaśiparamapāramiprāptairekaṃ pudgalaṃ sthāpayitvā yaduta āyuṣmantamānandam | [ASāh, 1 1.2]
tatra khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtiṃ sthaviramāmantrayate sma pratibhātu te subhūte bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ prajñāpāramitāmārabhya yathā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ prajñāpāramitā niryāyuriti | [ASāh, 1 2.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasyaitadabhavat kimayamāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ sthavira ātmīyena svakena prajñāpratibhānabalādhānena svakena prajñāpratibhānabalādhiṣṭhānena bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ prajñāpāramitāmupadekṣyati utāho buddhānubhāveneti | [ASāh, 1 3.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena āyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasya imamevaṃrūpaṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat yatkiṃcidāyuṣman śāriputra bhagavataḥ śrāvakā bhāṣante deśayanti upadiśanti udīrayanti prakāśayanti saṃprakāśayanti sa sarvastathāgatasya puruṣakāro veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 3.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ yo hi tathāgatena dharmo deśitaḥ tatra dharmadeśanāyāṃ śikṣamāṇāste tāṃ dharmatāṃ sākṣātkurvanti dhārayanti tāṃ dharmatāṃ sākṣātkṛtya dhārayitvā yadyadeva bhāṣante yadyadeva deśayanti yadyadeva upadiśanti yadyadevodīrayanti yadyadeva prakāśayanti yadyadeva saṃprakāśayanti sarvaṃ taddharmatayā aviruddham | [ASāh, 1 3.3]
tathāgatadharmadeśanāyā eva āyuṣman śāriputra eṣa niṣyandaḥ yatte kulaputrā upadiśantastāṃ dharmatāṃ dharmatayā na virodhayanti | [ASāh, 1 3.4]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena bhagavantametadavocat yadbhagavānevamāha pratibhātu te subhūte bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ prajñāpāramitāmārabhya yathā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ prajñāpāramitāṃ niryāyuriti | [ASāh, 1 4.1]
bodhisattvo bodhisattva iti yadidaṃ bhagavannucyate katamasyaitadbhagavan dharmasyādhivacanaṃ yaduta bodhisattva iti nāhaṃ bhagavaṃstaṃ dharmaṃ samanupaśyāmi yaduta bodhisattva iti | [ASāh, 1 4.2]
tamapyahaṃ bhagavan dharmaṃ na samanupaśyāmi yaduta prajñāpāramitā nāma | [ASāh, 1 4.3]
so 'haṃ bhagavan bodhisattvaṃ vā bodhisattvadharmaṃ vā avindan anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan prajñāpāramitām apyavindan anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan katamaṃ bodhisattvaṃ katamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāmavavadiṣyāmi anuśāsiṣyāmi api tu khalu punarbhagavan sacedevaṃ bhāṣyamāṇe deśyamāne upadiśyamāne bodhisattvasya cittaṃ nāvalīyate na saṃlīyate na viṣīdati na viṣādamāpadyate nāsya vipṛṣṭhībhavati mānasam na bhagnapṛṣṭhībhavati nottrasyati na saṃtrasyati na saṃtrāsamāpadyate eṣa eva bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāmanuśāsanīyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 4.4]
eṣaivāsya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 4.5]
eṣo 'vavādaḥ prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 4.6]
sacedevaṃ tiṣṭhati eṣaivāsyāvavādānuśāsanī | [ASāh, 1 4.7]
punaraparaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caratā prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāvayatā evaṃ śikṣitavyaṃ yathā asau śikṣyamāṇastenāpi bodhicittena na manyeta | [ASāh, 1 5.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi taccittamacittam | [ASāh, 1 5.2]
prakṛtiścittasya prabhāsvarā | [ASāh, 1 5.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte asti taccittaṃ yaccittamacittam evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat kiṃ punarāyuṣman śāriputra yā acittatā tatra acittatāyāmastitā vā nāstitā vā vidyate vā upalabhyate vā śāriputra āha na hyetadāyuṣman subhūte | [ASāh, 1 6.1]
subhūtirāha sacedāyuṣman śāriputra tatra acittatāyāmastitā vā nāstitā vā na vidyate vā nopalabhyate vā api nu te yukta eṣa paryanuyogo bhavati yadāyuṣmān śāriputra evamāha asti taccittaṃ yaccittamacittamiti evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kā punareṣā āyuṣman subhūte acittatā subhūtirāha avikārā āyuṣman śāriputra avikalpā acittatā | [ASāh, 1 6.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmate subhūtaye sādhukāramadāt sādhu sādhvāyuṣman subhūte | [ASāh, 1 7.1]
yathāpi nāma tvaṃ bhagavatā araṇāvihāriṇām agratāyāṃ nirdiṣṭo nirdiśasi | [ASāh, 1 7.2]
ataś ca bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'vinivartanīyo 'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodher upaparīkṣitavyaḥ avirahitaś ca bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyā veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 7.3]
śrāvakabhūmāv api śikṣitukāmena iyameva prajñāpāramitā śrotavyā udgrahītavyā dhārayitavyā vācayitavyā paryavāptavyā pravartayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 7.4]
ihaiva prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣitavyaṃ yogam āpattavyam | [ASāh, 1 7.5]
pratyekabuddhabhūmāv api śikṣitukāmena iyameva prajñāpāramitā śrotavyā udgrahītavyā dhārayitavyā vācayitavyā paryavāptavyā pravartayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 7.6]
ihaiva prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣitavyaṃ yogamāpattavyam | [ASāh, 1 7.7]
bodhisattvabhūmāv api śikṣitukāmena iyameva prajñāpāramitā śrotavyā udgrahītavyā dhārayitavyā vācayitavyā paryavāptavyā pravartayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 7.8]
ihaiva prajñāpāramitāyām upāyakauśalyasamanvāgatena sarvabodhisattvadharmasamudāgamāya yogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 7.9]
tatkasya hetoḥ ihaiva hi prajñāpāramitāyāṃ vistareṇa sarvabodhisattvadharmā upadiṣṭāḥ yatra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena śikṣitavyaṃ yogamāpattavyam | [ASāh, 1 7.10]
anuttarāyām api samyaksaṃbodhau śikṣitukāmena iyameva prajñāpāramitā śrotavyā udgrahītavyā dhārayitavyā vācayitavyā paryavāptavyā pravartayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 7.11]
ihaiva prajñāpāramitāyām upāyakauśalyasamanvāgatena sarvabuddhadharmasamudāgamāya yogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 7.12]
tatkasya hetoḥ ihaiva hi prajñāpāramitāyāṃ vistareṇa sarvabuddhadharmā upadiṣṭāḥ yatra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena śikṣitavyaṃ yogamāpattavyam | [ASāh, 1 7.13]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat yo 'haṃ bhagavan etadeva bodhisattvanāmadheyaṃ na vedmi nopalabhe na samanupaśyāmi prajñāpāramitām api na vedmi nopalabhe na samanupaśyāmi | [ASāh, 1 8.1]
so 'haṃ bhagavan etadeva bodhisattvanāmadheyam avindan anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan prajñāpāramitām api avindan anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan katamaṃ bodhisattvaṃ katamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāmavavadiṣyāmi anuśāsiṣyāmi etadeva bhagavan kaukṛtyaṃ syāt yo 'haṃ vastvavindan anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan nāmadheyamātreṇa āyavyayaṃ kuryāṃ yaduta bodhisattva iti | [ASāh, 1 8.2]
api tu khalu punarbhagavaṃstad api nāmadheyaṃ na sthitaṃ nāsthitaṃ na viṣṭhitaṃ nāviṣṭhitam | [ASāh, 1 8.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ avidyamānatvena tasya nāmadheyasya | [ASāh, 1 8.4]
evaṃ tannāmadheyaṃ na sthitaṃ nāsthitaṃ na viṣṭhitaṃ nāviṣṭhitam | [ASāh, 1 8.5]
sacedbodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya evaṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyāṃ cittaṃ nāvalīyate na saṃlīyate na viṣīdati na viṣādamāpadyate nāsya vipṛṣṭhībhavati mānasam na bhagnapṛṣṭhībhavati nottrasyati na saṃtrasyati na saṃtrāsamāpadyate | [ASāh, 1 8.6]
adhimucyate 'dhyāśayena avirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyā veditavyaḥ sthito 'vinivartanīyāyāṃ bodhisattvabhūmau susthito 'sthānayogena | [ASāh, 1 8.7]
punaraparaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caratā prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāvayatā na rūpe sthātavyaṃ na vedanāyāṃ na saṃjñāyāṃ na saṃskāreṣu na vijñāne sthātavyam | [ASāh, 1 8.8]
tatkasya hetoḥ sacedrūpe tiṣṭhati rūpābhisaṃskāre carati na carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 8.9]
evaṃ sacedvedanāyāṃ saṃjñāyāṃ saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 1 8.10]
sacedvijñāne tiṣṭhati vijñānābhisaṃskāre carati na carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 8.11]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi abhisaṃskāre caran prajñāpāramitāṃ parigṛhṇāti nāpi prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpadyate nāpi prajñāpāramitāṃ paripūrayate | [ASāh, 1 8.12]
aparipūryamāṇaḥ prajñāpāramitāṃ na niryāsyati sarvajñatāyām aparigṛhītaṃ parigṛhṇan | [ASāh, 1 8.13]
tatkasya hetoḥ rūpaṃ hi aparigṛhītaṃ prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 8.14]
evaṃ vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.15]
vijñānaṃ hi aparigṛhītaṃ prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 8.16]
yaś ca rūpasyāparigrahaḥ na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 8.17]
evaṃ yo vedanāyāḥ saṃjñāyāḥ saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 1 8.18]
yo vijñānasyāparigrahaḥ na tadvijñānam | [ASāh, 1 8.19]
sāpi prajñāpāramitā aparigṛhītā | [ASāh, 1 8.20]
evaṃ hyatra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caritavyam | [ASāh, 1 8.21]
ayaṃ ca bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya sarvadharmāparigṛhīto nāma samādhirvipulaḥ puraskṛtaḥ apramāṇaniyato 'sādhāraṇaḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.22]
sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhaiḥ sāpi sarvajñatā aparigṛhītā na hi nimittato grahītavyā | [ASāh, 1 8.23]
sacennimittato grahītavyā abhaviṣyat na ceha śreṇikaḥ parivrājakaḥ śraddhām alapsyata | [ASāh, 1 8.24]
tatra hi śreṇikaḥ parivrājakaḥ sarvajñajñāne adhimucya śraddhānusārī prādeśikena jñānenāvatīrṇaḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.25]
so 'vatīrya na rūpaṃ parigṛhṇīte | [ASāh, 1 8.26]
evaṃ na vedanāṃ na saṃjñāṃ na saṃskārān | [ASāh, 1 8.27]
na vijñānaṃ parigṛhṇīte | [ASāh, 1 8.28]
nāpi tatra prītisukhena tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.29]
nādhyātmaṃ rūpasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.30]
na bahirdhā rūpasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.31]
nādhyātmabahirdhā rūpasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.32]
nāpyanyatra rūpāttajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.33]
evaṃ nādhyātmaṃ vedanāyāḥ saṃjñāyāḥ saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 1 8.34]
nādhyātmaṃ vijñānasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.35]
na bahirdhā vijñānasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.36]
nādhyātmabahirdhā vijñānasya tajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.37]
nāpyanyatra vijñānāttajjñānaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 8.38]
atra padaparyāye śreṇikaḥ parivrājako 'dhimuktaḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.39]
so 'tra sarvatra śraddhānusārī sarvajñajñāne dharmatāṃ pramāṇīkṛtya evamadhimukta iti | [ASāh, 1 8.40]
tena na kaściddharmaḥ parigṛhītaḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.41]
nāpi sa kaściddharmo ya upalabdhaḥ yaṃ gṛhṇīyānmuñcedvā | [ASāh, 1 8.42]
sa nirvāṇam api na manyate | [ASāh, 1 8.43]
iyam api bhagavan bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā veditavyā yadrūpaṃ na parigṛhṇīte | [ASāh, 1 8.44]
evaṃ yadvedanāṃ saṃjñāṃ saṃskārān | [ASāh, 1 8.45]
yadvijñānaṃ na parigṛhṇīte | [ASāh, 1 8.46]
na cāntarā parinirvāti aparipūrṇair daśabhistathāgatabalaiś caturbhis tathāgatavaiśāradyair aṣṭādaśabhiś ca āveṇikairbuddhadharmaiḥ | [ASāh, 1 8.47]
tasmādiyam api bhagavan bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 8.48]
punaraparaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caratā prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāvayatā evam upaparīkṣitavyam evam upanidhyātavyam katamaiṣā prajñāpāramitā kasya caiṣā prajñāpāramitā kiṃ yo dharmo na vidyate nopalabhyate sā prajñāpāramiteti sacedevam upaparīkṣamāṇaḥ evamupanidhyāyan nāvalīyate na saṃlīyate na viṣīdati na viṣādamāpadyate nāsya vipṛṣṭhībhavati mānasam na bhagnapṛṣṭhībhavati nottrasyati na saṃtrasyati na saṃtrāsamāpadyate avirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitayā veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 9.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kiṃ kāraṇamāyuṣman subhūte avirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitayā veditavyaḥ yadā rūpameva virahitaṃ rūpasvabhāvena evaṃ yadā vedanaiva saṃjñaiva saṃskārā eva yadā vijñānameva virahitaṃ vijñānasvabhāvena yadā prajñāpāramitaiva virahitā prajñāpāramitāsvabhāvena yadā sarvajñataiva virahitā sarvajñatāsvabhāvena | [ASāh, 1 10.1]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat etametadāyuṣman śāriputra evam etat | [ASāh, 1 11.1]
rūpamevāyuṣman śāriputra virahitaṃ rūpasvabhāvena | [ASāh, 1 11.2]
evaṃ vedanaiva saṃjñaiva saṃskārā eva | [ASāh, 1 11.3]
vijñānamevāyuṣman śāriputra virahitaṃ vijñānasvabhāvena | [ASāh, 1 11.4]
prajñāpāramitaiva āyuṣman śāriputra virahitā prajñāpāramitāsvabhāvena | [ASāh, 1 11.5]
sarvajñataiva āyuṣman śāriputra virahitā sarvajñatāsvabhāvena | [ASāh, 1 11.6]
prajñāpāramitālakṣaṇenāpi prajñāpāramitā virahitā | [ASāh, 1 11.7]
lakṣaṇasvabhāvenāpi lakṣaṇaṃ virahitam | [ASāh, 1 11.8]
lakṣyasvabhāvenāpi lakṣyaṃ virahitam | [ASāh, 1 11.9]
svabhāvalakṣaṇenāpi svabhāvo virahitaḥ | [ASāh, 1 11.10]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte yo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'tra śikṣiṣyate sa niryāsyati sarvajñatāyām āyuṣmān subhūtirāha evametadāyuṣman śāriputra evam etat | [ASāh, 1 12.1]
yo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'tra śikṣiṣyate sa niryāsyati sarvajñatāyām | [ASāh, 1 12.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ ajātā hyanirjātā hyāyuṣman śāriputra sarvadharmāḥ | [ASāh, 1 12.3]
evaṃ carata āyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya sarvajñatā āsannībhavati | [ASāh, 1 12.4]
yathā yathā sarvajñatā āsannībhavati tathā tathā sattvaparipācanāya kāyacittapariśuddhirlakṣaṇapariśuddhiḥ buddhakṣetraśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 1 12.5]
buddhaiś ca samavadhānaṃ bhavati | [ASāh, 1 12.6]
evaṃ ca punarāyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran sarvajñatāyā āsannībhavati | [ASāh, 1 12.7]
punaraparamāyuṣmān subhūtir bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamārabhyaivamāha sacedrūpe carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.1]
sacedrūpanimitte carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.2]
sacedrūpaṃ nimittamiti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.3]
sa cedrūpasyotpāde carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.4]
sacedrūpasya nirodhe carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.5]
sacedrūpasya vināśe carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.6]
sacedrūpaṃ śūnyamiti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.7]
ahaṃ carāmīti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.8]
ahaṃ bodhisattva iti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.9]
ahaṃ bodhisattva iti hyupalambha eva sa carati | [ASāh, 1 13.10]
evaṃ saced vedanāyāṃ saṃjñāyāṃ saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 1 13.11]
sacedvijñāne carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.12]
sacedvijñānanimitte carati nimitte carati sacedvijñānaṃ nimittamiti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.13]
sacedvijñānasyotpāde carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.14]
sacedvijñānasya nirodhe carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.15]
sacedvijñānasya vināśe carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.16]
sacedvijñānaṃ śūnyamiti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.17]
ahaṃ carāmīti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.18]
ahaṃ bodhisattva iti carati nimitte carati | [ASāh, 1 13.19]
ahaṃ bodhisattva iti hyupalambha eva sa carati | [ASāh, 1 13.20]
sacetpunarasyaivaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ carati sa prajñāpāramitāyāṃ carati sa prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāvayatīti nimitta eva sa carati | [ASāh, 1 13.21]
ayaṃ bodhisattvo 'nupāyakuśalo veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 13.22]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kathaṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte caran bodhisattvo mahāsattvaścarati prajñāpāramitāyām evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat sacedāyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na rūpe carati na rūpanimitte carati na rūpaṃ nimittamiti carati na rūpasyotpāde carati na rūpasya nirodhe carati na rūpasya vināśe carati na rūpaṃ śūnyamiti carati nāhaṃ carāmīti carati nāhaṃ bodhisattva iti carati | [ASāh, 1 14.1]
evaṃ sacenna vedanāyāṃ na saṃjñāyāṃ na saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 1 14.2]
sacenna vijñāne carati na vijñānanimitte carati na vijñānaṃ nimittamiti carati na vijñānasyotpāde carati na vijñānasya nirodhe carati na vijñānasya vināśe carati na vijñānaṃ śūnyamiti carati nāhaṃ carāmīti carati nāhaṃ bodhisattva iti carati | [ASāh, 1 14.3]
sacetpunarnāsyaivaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ carati sa prajñāpāramitāyāṃ carati sa prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāvayatīti | [ASāh, 1 14.4]
evaṃ caran bodhisattvo mahāsattvaścarati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 14.5]
sa hi caraṃścarāmīti nopaiti na carāmīti nopaiti carāmi ca na carāmi ceti nopaiti naiva carāmi na na carāmīti nopaiti cariṣyāmīti nopaiti na cariṣyāmīti nopaiti cariṣyāmi ca na cariṣyāmi ceti nopaiti naiva cariṣyāmi na cariṣyāmīti nopaiti | [ASāh, 1 14.6]
tatkasya hetor nopaiti sarvadharmā hyanupagatā anupāttāḥ | [ASāh, 1 14.7]
ayamucyate sarvadharmānupādāno nāma samādhirbodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya vipulaḥ puraskṛto 'pramāṇaniyato 'sādhāraṇaḥ sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhaiḥ | [ASāh, 1 14.8]
anenaiva samādhinā viharan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ kṣipramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyate | [ASāh, 1 14.9]
buddhānubhāvena āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ sthavira evamāha vyākṛto 'yaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ pūrvakaistathāgatairarhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhairanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau yo 'nena samādhinā viharati | [ASāh, 1 15.1]
sa tam api samādhiṃ na samanupaśyati na ca tena samādhinā manyate ahaṃ samāhitaḥ ahaṃ samādhiṃ samāpatsye ahaṃ samādhiṃ samāpadye ahaṃ samādhisamāpannaḥ iti evaṃ tasya sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ na saṃvidyate | [ASāh, 1 15.2]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat katamenāyuṣman subhūte samādhinā viharan bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathāgatairarhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhairvyākriyate 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau śakyaḥ sa samādhirdarśayitum subhūtirāha no hīdamāyuṣman śāriputra | [ASāh, 1 16.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tam api hi sa kulaputraḥ samādhiṃ na jānāti na saṃjānīte | [ASāh, 1 16.2]
āyuṣmān śāriputra āha na jānāti na saṃjānīte ityāyuṣman subhūte vadasi āyuṣmān subhūtirāha na jānāti na saṃjānīte ityāyuṣman śāriputra vadāmi | [ASāh, 1 16.3]
tatkasya hetorna jānāti na saṃjānīte avidyamānatvena tasya samādhestaṃ samādhiṃ na jānāti na saṃjānīte | [ASāh, 1 16.4]
atha khalu bhagavān āyuṣmate subhūtaye sādhukāramadāt sādhu sādhu subhūte | [ASāh, 1 16.5]
evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 1 16.6]
yathāpi nāma tathāgatānubhāvena te pratibhāti tathāgatādhiṣṭhānenopadiśasi | [ASāh, 1 16.7]
evaṃ cātra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena śikṣitavyam | [ASāh, 1 16.8]
tatkasya hetoḥ evaṃ hi śikṣamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 16.9]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat evaṃ śikṣamāṇo bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣate evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 17.1]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat evaṃ śikṣamāṇo bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ katamasmin dharme śikṣate evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na kasmiṃściddharme śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 18.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi te śāriputra dharmāstathā saṃvidyante yathā bālapṛthagjanā aśrutavanto 'bhiniviṣṭāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.2]
āyuṣmān śāriputra āha kathaṃ tarhi te bhagavan saṃvidyante bhagavānāha yathā śāriputra na saṃvidyante tathā saṃvidyante evamavidyamānāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.3]
tenocyante avidyeti | [ASāh, 1 18.4]
tān bālapṛthagjanā aśrutavanto 'bhiniviṣṭāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.5]
tair asaṃvidyamānāḥ sarvadharmāḥ kalpitāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.6]
te tān kalpayitvā dvayorantayoḥ saktāḥ tān dharmānna jānanti na paśyanti | [ASāh, 1 18.7]
tasmātte 'saṃvidyamānān sarvadharmān kalpayanti | [ASāh, 1 18.8]
kalpayitvā dvāvantāvabhiniviśante abhiniviśya tannidānamupalambhaṃ niśritya atītān dharmān kalpayanti anāgatān dharmān kalpayanti pratyutpannān dharmān kalpayanti te kalpayitvā nāmarūpe 'bhiniviṣṭāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.9]
tair asaṃvidyamānāḥ sarvadharmāḥ kalpitāḥ | [ASāh, 1 18.10]
te tān asaṃvidyamānān sarvadharmān kalpayanto yathābhūtaṃ mārgaṃ na jānanti na paśyanti | [ASāh, 1 18.11]
yathābhūtaṃ mārgam ajānanto 'paśyanto na niryānti traidhātukāt na budhyante bhūtakoṭim | [ASāh, 1 18.12]
tena te bālā iti saṃjñāṃ gacchanti | [ASāh, 1 18.13]
te satyaṃ dharmaṃ na śraddadhati | [ASāh, 1 18.14]
na khalu punaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ kaṃciddharmamabhiniviśante | [ASāh, 1 18.15]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat evaṃ śikṣamāṇo bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣate bhagavānāha evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyām api na śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 19.1]
evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvadharmeṣu śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 19.2]
evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣate sarvajñatāyā āsannībhavati sarvajñatāyāṃ niryāsyati | [ASāh, 1 19.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat yo bhagavan evaṃ paripṛcchet kimayaṃ māyāpuruṣāḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣiṣyate sarvajñatāyā āsannībhaviṣyati sarvajñatāyāṃ niryāsyatīti tasya bhagavan evaṃ paripṛcchataḥ kathaṃ nirdeṣṭavyaṃ syāt evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat tena hi subhūte tvāmevātra pratiprakṣyāmi | [ASāh, 1 20.1]
yathā te kṣamate tathā vyākuryāḥ | [ASāh, 1 20.2]
sādhu bhagavannityāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [ASāh, 1 20.3]
bhagavānetadavocat tatkiṃ manyase subhūte anyā sā māyā anyattadrūpam anyā sā māyā anyā sā vedanā | [ASāh, 1 20.4]
anyā sā saṃjñā anye te saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 20.5]
anyā sā māyā anyattadvijñānam subhūtirāha na hyetadbhagavan | [ASāh, 1 20.6]
na hi bhagavan anyā sā māyā anyattadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 20.7]
rūpameva bhagavan māyā māyaiva rūpam | [ASāh, 1 20.8]
na hi bhagavan anyā sā māyā anyā sā vedanā anyā sā saṃjñā anye te saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 20.9]
vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārā eva bhagavan māyā māyaiva vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 20.10]
na bhagavan anyā sā māyā anyattadvijñānam | [ASāh, 1 20.11]
vijñānameva bhagavan māyā māyaiva vijñānam | [ASāh, 1 20.12]
bhagavānāha tatkiṃ manyase subhūte atraiṣāṃ saṃjñā samajñā prajñaptirvyavahāraḥ pañcasūpādānaskandheṣu yaduta bodhisattva iti evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat evametadbhagavan evametatsugata | [ASāh, 1 21.1]
tena hi bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣamāṇena māyāpuruṣeṇeva śikṣitavyaṃ bhavatyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [ASāh, 1 21.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ sa eva hi bhagavan māyāpuruṣo dhārayitavyo yaduta pañcopādānaskandhāḥ | [ASāh, 1 21.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi bhagavan māyopamaṃ rūpamuktaṃ bhagavatā | [ASāh, 1 21.4]
yacca rūpaṃ tatṣaḍindriyaṃ te pañca skandhāḥ | [ASāh, 1 21.5]
tathā hi bhagavan māyopamā vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārā uktāḥ | [ASāh, 1 21.6]
tathā hi bhagavan māyopamaṃ vijñānamuktaṃ bhagavatā | [ASāh, 1 21.7]
yacca vijñānaṃ tatṣaḍindriyaṃ te pañca skandhāḥ | [ASāh, 1 21.8]
mā bhagavan navayānasamprasthitā bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imaṃ nirdeśaṃ śrutvā uttrasiṣuḥ saṃtrasiṣuḥ saṃtrāsamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 1 21.9]
bhagavānāha yadi subhūte navayānasamprasthitā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ pāpamitrahastagatā bhaviṣyanti uttrasiṣyanti saṃtrasiṣyanti saṃtrāsamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 1 21.10]
atha cetsubhūte navayānasamprasthitā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ kalyāṇamitrahastagatā bhaviṣyanti nottrasiṣyanti na saṃtrasiṣyanti na saṃtrāsamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 1 21.11]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat kāni punarbhagavan bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya kalyāṇamitrāṇi veditavyāni bhagavānāha ya enaṃ pāramitāsu avavadanti anuśāsati | [ASāh, 1 22.1]
ye 'smai mārakarmāṇyupadiśanti | [ASāh, 1 22.2]
evaṃ māradoṣā boddhavyāḥ ime māradoṣāḥ | [ASāh, 1 22.3]
evaṃ mārakarmāṇi boddhavyāni imāni mārakarmāṇi | [ASāh, 1 22.4]
tāni tvayā buddhvā vivarjayitavyānīti | [ASāh, 1 22.5]
imāni subhūte bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhasya mahāyānasamprasthitasya mahāyānasamārūḍhasya kalyāṇamitrāṇi veditavyāni | [ASāh, 1 22.6]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat yadbhagavānevamāha imāni subhūte bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhasya mahāyānasamprasthitasya mahāyānasamārūḍhasya kalyāṇamitrāṇi veditavyānīti | [ASāh, 1 22.7]
yacca bodhisattvo mahāsattva iti bhagavannucyate tatra bodhisattva iti bhagavan kaḥ padārtha evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat apadārthaḥ subhūte bodhisattvapadārthaḥ | [ASāh, 1 22.8]
tatkasya hetoḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ hi subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'saktatāyāṃ śikṣate | [ASāh, 1 22.9]
sarvadharmāṇāṃ hi subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nubodhanārthena asaktatāyāmanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyate | [ASāh, 1 22.10]
bodhyarthena tu subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate | [ASāh, 1 22.11]
subhūtirāha yatpunarbhagavānevamāha bodhisattvo mahāsattva iti kena kāraṇena bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate bhagavānāha mahataḥ sattvarāśermahataḥ sattvanikāyasya agratāṃ kārayiṣyati tenārthena bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate | [ASāh, 1 22.12]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat mamāpi bhagavan pratibhāti yenārthena bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate | [ASāh, 1 23.1]
bhagavānāha pratibhātu te śāriputra yasyedānīṃ kālaṃ manyase | [ASāh, 1 23.2]
āyuṣmān śāriputra āha mahatyā ātmadṛṣṭyāḥ sattvadṛṣṭyāḥ jīvadṛṣṭyāḥ pudgaladṛṣṭyāḥ bhavadṛṣṭyāḥ vibhavadṛṣṭyāḥ ucchedadṛṣṭyāḥ śāśvatadṛṣṭyāḥ svakāyadṛṣṭyāḥ etāsāmevamādyānāṃ dṛṣṭīnāṃ prahāṇāya dharmaṃ deśayiṣyatīti tenārthena bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate | [ASāh, 1 23.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat mamāpi bhagavan pratibhāti yenārthena bodhisattvo mahāsattva ityucyate | [ASāh, 1 23.4]
bhagavānāha pratibhātu te subhūte yasyedānīṃ kālaṃ manyase | [ASāh, 1 23.5]
subhūtirāha bodhisattvo mahāsattva iti bhagavannucyate | [ASāh, 1 23.6]
yad api tadbhagavan bodhicittaṃ sarvajñatācittamanāsravaṃ cittamasamaṃ cittaṃ asamasamaṃ cittamasādhāraṇaṃ sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhaiḥ tatrāpi citte asakto 'paryāpannaḥ | [ASāh, 1 23.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi tatsarvajñatācittam anāsravam aparyāpannaṃ tat yad api tatsarvajñatācittam anāsravam aparyāpannam | [ASāh, 1 23.8]
tatrāpi citte asakto 'paryāpannaḥ | [ASāh, 1 23.9]
tenārthena bodhisattvo mahāsattva iti saṃkhyāṃ gacchati | [ASāh, 1 23.10]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kena kāraṇena āyuṣman subhūte tatrāpi citte asakto 'paryāpannaḥ subhūtirāha acittatvādāyuṣman śāriputra tatrāpi citte asakto 'paryāpannaḥ | [ASāh, 1 24.1]
śāriputra āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte asti taccittaṃ yaccittamacittam subhūtirāha kiṃ punarāyuṣman śāriputra tatra acittatāyāmastitā vā nāstitā vā vidyate vā upalabhyate vā śāriputra āha no hīdamāyuṣman subhūte | [ASāh, 1 25.1]
subhūtirāha tadyadi āyuṣman śāriputra tatra acittatāyāmastitā vā nāstitā vā na vidyate vā nopalabhyate vā tatkatham āyuṣmān śāriputra evamāha asti taccittaṃ yaccittamacittamiti śāriputra āha sādhu sādhu āyuṣman subhūte | [ASāh, 1 25.2]
yathāpi nāma tvaṃ bhagavatā araṇāvihāriṇāmagratāyāṃ nirdiṣṭo nirdiśasi | [ASāh, 1 25.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputro bhagavantametadavocat mahāsattvo mahāsattva iti yadidaṃ bhagavannucyate mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhaḥ sa sattvaḥ | [ASāh, 1 26.1]
mahāyānasamprasthito mahāyānasamārūḍhaś ca sa sattvaḥ | [ASāh, 1 26.2]
tasmātsa mahāsattvo mahāsattva iti saṃkhyāṃ gacchati | [ASāh, 1 26.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddho mahāyānasaṃnaddha iti yadidaṃ bhagavannucyate kiyatā bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddho bhavati bhagavānāha iha subhūte bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyaivaṃ bhavati aprameyā mayā sattvāḥ parinirvāpayitavyā iti | [ASāh, 1 27.1]
asaṃkhyeyā mayā sattvāḥ parinirvāpayitavyā iti | [ASāh, 1 27.2]
na ca te santi yairye parinirvāpayitavyā iti | [ASāh, 1 27.3]
sa tāṃstāvataḥ sattvān parinirvāpayati | [ASāh, 1 27.4]
na ca sa kaścitsattvo yaḥ parinirvṛto yena ca parinirvāpito bhavati | [ASāh, 1 27.5]
tatkasya hetoḥ dharmataiṣā subhūte dharmāṇāṃ māyādharmatāmupādāya syāt | [ASāh, 1 27.6]
yathāpi nāma subhūte dakṣo māyākāro vā māyākārāntevāsī vā caturmahāpathe mahāntaṃ janakāyamabhinirmimīte | [ASāh, 1 27.7]
abhinirmāya tasyaiva mahato janakāyasyāntardhānaṃ kuryāt | [ASāh, 1 27.8]
tatkiṃ manyase subhūte api nu tatra kenacitkaściddhato vā mṛto vā nāśito vā antarhito vā subhūtirāha no hīdaṃ bhagavan | [ASāh, 1 27.9]
bhagavānāha evameva subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'prameyānasaṃkhyeyān sattvān parinirvāpayati | [ASāh, 1 27.10]
na ca sa kaścitsattvo yaḥ parinirvṛto yena ca parinirvāpito bhavati | [ASāh, 1 27.11]
sacedbodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ nirdeśamevaṃ nirdiśyamānaṃ śrutvā nottrasyati na saṃtrasyati na saṃtrāsamāpadyate iyatā ayaṃ subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddho veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 27.12]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat yathāhaṃ bhagavan bhagavato bhāṣitasyārthamājānāmi tathā asaṃnāhasaṃnaddho batāyaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 28.1]
bhagavānāha evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 1 28.2]
asaṃnāhasaṃnaddho batāyaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 28.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ akṛtā hi subhūte sarvajñatā avikṛtā anabhisaṃskṛtā | [ASāh, 1 28.4]
te 'pi sattvā akṛtā avikṛtā anabhisaṃskṛtāḥ yeṣāṃ sattvānāmarthāya ayaṃ saṃnāhasaṃnaddhaḥ | [ASāh, 1 28.5]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat evametadbhagavan evametatsugata | [ASāh, 1 29.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi bhagavan rūpamabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 1 29.2]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 29.3]
tathā hi bhagavan vijñānamabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 1 29.4]
rūpatathatāpi bhagavan abaddhā amuktā | [ASāh, 1 29.5]
evaṃ vedanātathatāpi saṃjñātathatāpi saṃskāratathatāpi | [ASāh, 1 29.6]
vijñānatathatāpi bhagavan abaddhā amuktā | [ASāh, 1 29.7]
atha khalvāyuṣmān pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat rūpamāyuṣman subhūte abaddhamamuktamiti vadasi | [ASāh, 1 30.1]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 30.2]
vijñānamāyuṣman subhūte abaddhamamuktamiti vadasi | [ASāh, 1 30.3]
rūpatathatāpi āyuṣman subhūte abaddhā amukteti vadasi | [ASāh, 1 30.4]
evaṃ vedanātathatāpi saṃjñātathatāpi saṃskāratathatāpi | [ASāh, 1 30.5]
vijñānatathatāpyāyuṣman subhūte abaddhā amukteti vadasi | [ASāh, 1 30.6]
atha katamattadāyuṣman subhūte rūpaṃ yadrūpamabaddhamamuktamiti vadasi evaṃ katamā sā vedanā katamā sā saṃjñā katame te saṃskārāḥ katamattadāyuṣman subhūte vijñānaṃ yadvijñānamabaddhamamuktamiti vadasi katamā sā āyuṣman subhūte rūpatathatā yā rūpatathatāpyabaddhā amukteti vadasi evaṃ katamā sā vedanātathatā saṃjñātathatā saṃskāratathatā katamā sā āyuṣman subhūte vijñānatathatā yā vijñānatathatāpyabaddhā amukteti vadasi evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ pūrṇaṃ maitrāyaṇīputrametadavocat yadāyuṣman pūrṇa māyāpuruṣasya rūpaṃ tadabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 1 30.7]
evaṃ yā māyāpuruṣasya vedanā yā māyāpuruṣasya saṃjñā ye māyāpuruṣasya saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 30.8]
yadāyuṣman pūrṇa māyāpuruṣasya vijñānaṃ tadabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 1 30.9]
yā āyuṣman pūrṇa māyāpuruṣasya rūpatathatā sā abaddhā amuktā | [ASāh, 1 30.10]
evaṃ yā māyāpuruṣasya vedanātathatā saṃjñātathatā saṃskāratathatā | [ASāh, 1 30.11]
yā āyuṣman pūrṇa māyāpuruṣasya vijñānatathatā sā abaddhā amuktā | [ASāh, 1 30.12]
tatkasya hetoḥ asadbhūtatvādabaddhā amuktā viviktatvādabaddhā amuktā anutpannatvādabaddhā amuktā | [ASāh, 1 30.13]
ayaṃ sa bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhasya mahāyānasamprasthitasya mahāyānasamārūḍhasya mahāsaṃnāho 'saṃnāhaḥ | [ASāh, 1 30.14]
evamukte āyuṣmān pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputrastūṣṇīmabhūt | [ASāh, 1 30.15]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat evaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhaḥ san mahāyānasamprasthito mahāyānasamārūḍho bhavati | [ASāh, 1 31.1]
katamacca tanmahāyānam kathaṃ vā tatsamprasthito veditavyaḥ kuto vā tanmahāyānaṃ niryāsyati kena vā tanmahāyānaṃ samprasthitam kva vā tanmahāyānaṃ sthāsyati ko vā anena mahāyānena niryāsyati evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat mahāyānamiti subhūte aprameyatāyā etadadhivacanam | [ASāh, 1 31.2]
aprameyamiti subhūte apramāṇatvena | [ASāh, 1 31.3]
yad api subhūte evaṃ vadasi kathaṃ vā tatsamprasthito veditavyaḥ kuto vā tanmahāyānaṃ niryāsyati kena vā tanmahāyānaṃ samprasthitam kva vā tanmahāyānaṃ sthāsyati ko vā anena mahāyānena niryāsyatīti pāramitābhiḥ samprasthitaḥ | [ASāh, 1 31.4]
traidhātukānniryāsyati | [ASāh, 1 31.5]
yenārambaṇaṃ tena samprasthitam | [ASāh, 1 31.6]
sarvajñatāyāṃ sthāsyati | [ASāh, 1 31.7]
bodhisattvo mahāsattvo niryāsyati api tu khalu punarna kutaścinniryāsyati | [ASāh, 1 31.8]
na kenāpi samprasthitam | [ASāh, 1 31.9]
na kvacitsthāsyati | [ASāh, 1 31.10]
api tu sthāsyati sarvajñatāyām asthānayogena | [ASāh, 1 31.11]
nāpi kaścittena mahāyānena niryāto nāpi niryāsyati nāpi niryāti | [ASāh, 1 31.12]
tatkasya hetoḥ yaś ca niryāyāt yena ca niryāyāt ubhāvetau dharmau na vidyete nopalabhyete | [ASāh, 1 31.13]
evamavidyamāneṣu sarvadharmeṣu katamo dharmaḥ katamena dharmeṇa niryāsyati evaṃ hi subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo mahāyānasaṃnaddho mahāyānasamprasthito mahāyānasamārūḍho bhavati | [ASāh, 1 31.14]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat mahāyānaṃ mahāyānamiti bhagavannucyate | [ASāh, 1 32.1]
sadevamānuṣāsuraṃ lokamabhibhavanniryāsyati ākāśasamatayā atimahattayā tanmahāyānam | [ASāh, 1 32.2]
yathā ākāśe aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmavakāśaḥ evameva bhagavan asmin yāne aprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmavakāśaḥ | [ASāh, 1 32.3]
anena bhagavan paryāyeṇa mahāyānamidaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [ASāh, 1 32.4]
naivāsyāgamo dṛśyate naivāsya nirgamo dṛśyate nāpyasya sthānaṃ saṃvidyate | [ASāh, 1 32.5]
evamasya bhagavan mahāyānasya naiva pūrvānta upalabhyate nāpyaparānta upalabhyate nāpi madhya upalabhyate | [ASāh, 1 32.6]
atha samaṃ bhagavaṃstadyānam | [ASāh, 1 32.7]
tasmānmahāyānaṃ mahāyānamityucyate | [ASāh, 1 32.8]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmate subhūtaye sādhukāramadāt sādhu sādhu subhūte | [ASāh, 1 32.9]
evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 1 32.10]
evaṃ mahāyānamidaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [ASāh, 1 32.11]
atra śikṣitvā bodhisattvairmahāsattvaiḥ sarvajñatā anuprāptā anuprāpsyate anuprāpyate ca | [ASāh, 1 32.12]
atha khalvāyuṣmān pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputro bhagavantametadavocat ayaṃ bhagavan subhūtiḥ sthaviraḥ prajñāpāramitāyāḥ kṛtaśo 'dhīṣṭo mahāyānamupadeṣṭavyaṃ manyate | [ASāh, 1 33.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat nāhaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitāṃ vyatikramya mahāyānamavocam | [ASāh, 1 33.2]
bhagavānāha no hīdaṃ subhūte | [ASāh, 1 33.3]
anulomatvaṃ subhūte prajñāpāramitāyā mahāyānamupadiśasi | [ASāh, 1 33.4]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat buddhānubhāvādbhagavan | [ASāh, 1 33.5]
api nu khalu punarbhagavan pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti aparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti | [ASāh, 1 33.6]
tatkasya hetornopaiti rūpāparyantatayā hi bodhisattvāparyantatā veditavyā evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 33.7]
vijñānāparyantatayā hi bodhisattvāparyantatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 33.8]
rūpaṃ bodhisattva iti nopaiti | [ASāh, 1 33.9]
idam api na vidyate nopalabhyate | [ASāh, 1 33.10]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 1 33.11]
vijñānaṃ bodhisattva iti nopaiti idam api na vidyate nopalabhyate | [ASāh, 1 33.12]
evaṃ bhagavan sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ bodhisattvadharmam anupalabhamāno nāhaṃ bhagavan taṃ dharmaṃ samanupaśyāmi yasyaitannāmadheyaṃ yaduta bodhisattva iti | [ASāh, 1 33.13]
prajñāpāramitām api na samanupaśyāmi nopalabhe | [ASāh, 1 33.14]
sarvajñatām api na samanupaśyāmi nopalabhe | [ASāh, 1 33.15]
so 'haṃ bhagavan sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ taṃ dharmam anupalabhamāno 'samanupaśyan katamaṃ dharmaṃ katamena dharmeṇa katamasmin dharme 'vavadiṣyāmi anuśāsiṣyāmi buddha iti bhagavan nāmadheyamātram etat | [ASāh, 1 33.16]
bodhisattva iti bhagavan nāmadheyamātram etat | [ASāh, 1 33.17]
prajñāpāramiteti bhagavan nāmadheyamātram etat | [ASāh, 1 33.18]
tacca nāmadheyam anabhinirvṛttam | [ASāh, 1 33.19]
yathā ātmā ātmeti ca bhagavannucyate atyantatayā ca bhagavannanabhinirvṛtta ātmā | [ASāh, 1 33.20]
evamasvabhāvānāṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ katamattadrūpaṃ yad agrāhyam anabhinirvṛttam katame te vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ katamattadvijñānaṃ yad agrāhyam anabhinirvṛttam evameteṣāṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ yā asvabhāvatā sā anabhinirvṛttiḥ | [ASāh, 1 33.21]
yā ca sarvadharmāṇām anabhinirvṛttirna te dharmāḥ | [ASāh, 1 33.22]
tat kim anabhinirvṛttim anabhinirvṛttyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāmavavadiṣyāmyanuśāsiṣyāmi na cānyatra bhagavan anabhinirvṛttitaḥ sarvadharmā vā buddhadharmā vā bodhisattvadharmā vā upalabhyante yo vā bodhāya caret | [ASāh, 1 33.23]
sacedbhagavan evaṃ bhāṣyamāṇe evaṃ deśyamāne evamupadiśyamāne bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya cittaṃ nāvalīyate na saṃlīyate na viṣīdati na viṣādamāpadyate nāsya vipṛṣṭhībhavati mānasaṃ na bhagnapṛṣṭhībhavati nottrasyati na saṃtrasyati na saṃtrāsamāpadyate evaṃ veditavyam caratyayaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 1 33.24]
bhāvayatyayaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 1 33.25]
upaparīkṣate 'yaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 1 33.26]
upanidhyāyatyayaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāmiti | [ASāh, 1 33.27]
tatkasya hetoḥ yasmin hi samaye bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ imān dharmān prajñāpāramitāyāṃ vyupaparīkṣate tasmin samaye na rūpamupaiti na rūpamupagacchati na rūpasyotpādaṃ samanupaśyati na rūpasya nirodhaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 33.28]
evaṃ na vedanāṃ na saṃjñāṃ na saṃskārān | [ASāh, 1 33.29]
na vijñānamupaiti na vijñānamupagacchati na vijñānasyotpādaṃ samanupaśyati na vijñānasya nirodhaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 33.30]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi yo rūpasyānutpādo na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 33.31]
yo rūpasyāvyayo na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 33.32]
ityanutpādaś ca rūpaṃ ca advayametad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.33]
ityavyayaś ca rūpaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.34]
yatpunaretaducyate rūpamiti advayasyaiṣā gaṇanā kṛtā | [ASāh, 1 33.35]
evaṃ tathā hi yo vedanāyāḥ saṃjñāyāḥ saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 1 33.36]
tathā hi yo vijñānasyānutpādo na tadvijñānam yo vijñānasyāvyayo na tadvijñānam | [ASāh, 1 33.37]
ityanutpādaś ca vijñānaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.38]
ityavyayaś ca vijñānaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.39]
yatpunaretaducyate vijñānamiti advayasyaiṣā gaṇanā kṛtā | [ASāh, 1 33.40]
evaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sarvākāraṃ sarvadharmān vyupaparīkṣamāṇaḥ tasmin samaye na rūpamupaiti na rūpamupagacchati na rūpasyotpādaṃ samanupaśyati na rūpasya nirodhaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 33.41]
evaṃ na vedanāṃ na saṃjñāṃ na saṃskārān | [ASāh, 1 33.42]
na vijñānamupaiti na vijñānamupagacchati na vijñānasyotpādaṃ samanupaśyati na vijñānasya nirodhaṃ samanupaśyati | [ASāh, 1 33.43]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi yo rūpasyānutpādo na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 33.44]
yo rūpasyāvyayo na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 1 33.45]
ityanutpādaś ca rūpaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.46]
ityavyayaśca rūpaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.47]
yatpunaretaducyate rūpamiti advayasyaiṣā gaṇanā kṛtā | [ASāh, 1 33.48]
evaṃ tathā hi yo vedanāyāḥ saṃjñāyāḥ saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 1 33.49]
tathā hi yo vijñānasyānutpādo na tadvijñānam yo vijñānasyāvyayo na tadvijñānam | [ASāh, 1 33.50]
ityanutpādaś ca vijñānaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.51]
ityavyayaś ca vijñānaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 1 33.52]
yatpunaretaducyate vijñānamiti advayasyaiṣā gaṇanā kṛtā | [ASāh, 1 33.53]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat tena hi yathāhamāyuṣmataḥ subhūterbhāṣitasyārthamājānāmi tathā bodhisattvo 'pyanutpādaḥ | [ASāh, 1 34.1]
yadi ca āyuṣman subhūte bodhisattvo 'pyanutpādaḥ kiṃ bodhisattvo duṣkaracārikāṃ carati yāni vā tāni sattvānāṃ kṛtaśo duḥkhānyutsahate pratyanubhavitum evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat nāhamāyuṣman śāriputra icchāmi bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvaṃ duṣkaracārikāṃ carantam nāpi sa bodhisattvo mahāsattvo yo duṣkarasaṃjñayā carati | [ASāh, 1 34.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi āyuṣman śāriputra duṣkarasaṃjñāṃ janayitvā śakyo 'prameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmarthaḥ kartum | [ASāh, 1 34.3]
api tu sukhasaṃjñāmeva kṛtvā | [ASāh, 1 34.4]
sarvasattvānāmantike mātṛsaṃjñāṃ pitṛsaṃjñāṃ putrasaṃjñāṃ duhitṛsaṃjñāṃ kṛtvā strīpuruṣeṣu | [ASāh, 1 34.5]
evametāḥ saṃjñāḥ kṛtvā bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bodhisattvacārikāṃ carati | [ASāh, 1 34.6]
tasmānmātṛsaṃjñā pitṛsaṃjñā putrasaṃjñā duhitṛsaṃjñā bodhisattvena mahāsattvena sarvasattvānāmantike yāvadātmasaṃjñā utpādayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 34.7]
yathā ātmā sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ sarvaduḥkhebhyo mocayitavyaḥ evaṃ sarvasattvāḥ sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ sarvaduḥkhebhyo mocayitavyā iti | [ASāh, 1 34.8]
evaṃ ca sarvasattveṣu saṃjñā utpādayitavyā mayaite sarvasattvā na parityaktavyāḥ | [ASāh, 1 34.9]
mayaite sarvasattvāḥ parimocayitavyā aparimāṇato duḥkhaskandhāt | [ASāh, 1 34.10]
na ca mayaiteṣu cittapradoṣa utpādayitavya antaśaḥ śataśo 'pi chidyamāneneti | [ASāh, 1 34.11]
evaṃ hi bodhisattvena mahāsattvena cittamutpādayitavyam sa ced evaṃcitto vihariṣyati na duṣkarasaṃjñī cariṣyati na duṣkarasaṃjñī vihariṣyati | [ASāh, 1 34.12]
punaraparamāyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena evaṃ cittamutpādayitavyam yathā sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvamātmā na vidyate nopalabhyate evaṃ sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ sarvadharmā na saṃvidyante nopalabhyante | [ASāh, 1 34.13]
evamādhyātmikabāhyeṣu sarvadharmeṣu saṃjñā utpādayitavyā | [ASāh, 1 34.14]
saced evaṃcittaścariṣyati na duṣkarasaṃjñī cariṣyati na duṣkarasaṃjñī vihariṣyati | [ASāh, 1 34.15]
yadapyāyuṣman śāriputra evamāha anutpādo bodhisattvo iti | [ASāh, 1 34.16]
evametadāyuṣman śāriputra evam etat | [ASāh, 1 34.17]
anutpādo bodhisattva iti | [ASāh, 1 34.18]
śāriputra āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte bodhisattva evānutpādaḥ utāho bodhisattvadharmā apyanutpādaḥ subhūtirāha bodhisattvadharmā api āyuṣman śāriputra anutpādaḥ śāriputra āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte bodhisattvadharmā evānutpādaḥ utāho sarvajñatāpyanutpādaḥ subhūtirāha sarvajñatāpyāyuṣman śāriputra anutpādaḥ | [ASāh, 1 35.1]
āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte sarvajñataivānutpādaḥ utāho sarvajñatādharmā apyanutpādaḥ āha sarvajñatādharmā apyāyuṣman śāriputra anutpādaḥ | [ASāh, 1 35.2]
āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte sarvajñatādharmā evānutpādaḥ utāho pṛthagjano 'pyanutpādaḥ āha pṛthagjano 'pyāyuṣman śāriputra anutpādaḥ | [ASāh, 1 35.3]
āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte pṛthagjana evānutpādaḥ utāho pṛthagjanadharmā apyanutpādaḥ āha pṛthagjanadharmā apyāyuṣman śāriputra anutpādaḥ | [ASāh, 1 35.4]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat yadyāyuṣman subhūte bodhisattvo 'pyanutpādaḥ bodhisattvadharmā apyanutpādaḥ sarvajñatāpyanutpādaḥ sarvajñatādharmā apyanutpādaḥ pṛthagjano 'pyanutpādaḥ pṛthagjanadharmā apyanutpādaḥ nanvāyuṣman subhūte anuprāptaiva ayatnena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena sarvajñatā bhavati | [ASāh, 1 35.5]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat nāhamāyuṣman śāriputra anutpannasya dharmasya prāptimicchāmi nāpyabhisamayam | [ASāh, 1 35.6]
nāpyanutpannena dharmeṇa anutpannā prāptiḥ prāpyate | [ASāh, 1 35.7]
āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte anutpannena dharmeṇa anutpannā prāptiḥ prāpyate utāho utpannena dharmeṇa anutpannā prāptiḥ prāpyate āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman śāriputra anutpanno dharma utpannaḥ utāho anutpanna eva dharmo 'nutpannaḥ āha kiṃ punarāyuṣman subhūte utpāda eva dharmo 'nutpādaḥ utāho anutpādo dharma utpādaḥ āha utpādo dharmo 'nutpādo dharma ityāyuṣman śāriputra na pratibhāti jalpitum | [ASāh, 1 35.8]
āha anutpādo 'pi te āyuṣman subhūte pratibhāti jalpitum | [ASāh, 1 35.9]
āha anutpāda evāyuṣman śāriputra jalpaḥ | [ASāh, 1 35.10]
anutpāda eva āyuṣman śāriputra pratibhāti | [ASāh, 1 35.11]
anutpāda eva āyuṣman śāriputra pratibhānam | [ASāh, 1 35.12]
evamevāyuṣman śāriputra atyantaṃ pratibhāti | [ASāh, 1 35.13]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat dhārmakathikānāmāyuṣmān subhūtiragratāyāṃ sthāpitavyaḥ | [ASāh, 1 36.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hyāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ sthaviro yato yata eva paripraśnīkriyate tatastata eva niḥsarati dharmatāyāś ca na calati tāṃ ca dharmatāṃ na virodhayati | [ASāh, 1 36.2]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat dharmataiṣā āyuṣman śāriputra bhagavataḥ śrāvakāṇām aniśritadharmāṇām | [ASāh, 1 36.3]
te yato yata eva paripraśnīkriyante tatastata eva niḥsaranti dharmatāṃ ca na virodhayanti dharmatāyāś ca na vyativartante | [ASāh, 1 36.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ yathāpi nāma aniśritatvāt sarvadharmāṇām | [ASāh, 1 36.5]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat sādhu sādhu āyuṣman subhūte | [ASāh, 1 36.6]
katamaiṣā sarvadharmāniśritapāramitā bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām subhūtirāha prajñāpāramitaiva āyuṣman śāriputra sārvayānikī sarvadharmāniśritatayā sarvadharmāniśritapāramitā ca | [ASāh, 1 36.7]
iti hi yasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya evaṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāmevaṃ deśyamānāyām evam upadiśyamānāyāṃ na bhavati cittasya avalīnatvam na bhavati kāṅkṣāyitatvam na bhavati dhandhāyitatvam na bhavati cittasyānyathātvam veditavyam ayaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvo viharatyanena prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa avirahitaścānena manasikāreṇeti | [ASāh, 1 36.8]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmataṃ subhūtimetadavocat kathamāyuṣman subhūte avirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'virahito manasikāreṇa bhavati yaḥ prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa viharati yadi hyāyuṣman subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'virahito manasikāreṇa bhavati evaṃ sa virahitaḥ prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa bhavati | [ASāh, 1 37.1]
yadi ca āyuṣman subhūte avirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa bhavati evaṃ sa virahito manasikāreṇa bhavati | [ASāh, 1 37.2]
yadi ca āyuṣman subhūte manasikāreṇāvirahito bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ avirahita eva prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa bhavati | [ASāh, 1 37.3]
evaṃ sati sarvasattvā apyavirahitā bhaviṣyanti prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa | [ASāh, 1 37.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ sarvasattvā api hyavirahitā manasikāreṇa viharanti | [ASāh, 1 37.5]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat sādhu sādhu āyuṣman śāriputra | [ASāh, 1 38.1]
api tu upālapsye tvā | [ASāh, 1 38.2]
artha eva tvāyuṣmatā śāriputreṇa bhūtapadābhidhānena parigṛhītaḥ | [ASāh, 1 38.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ sattvāsvabhāvatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikārāsvabhāvatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.4]
sattvāsadbhāvatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikārāsadbhāvatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.5]
sattvaviviktatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikāraviviktatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.6]
sattvācintyatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikārācintyatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.7]
sattvānabhisaṃbodhanatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikārānabhisaṃbodhanatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.8]
sattvāyathābhūtārthābhisaṃbodhanatayā āyuṣman śāriputra manasikārāyathābhūtārthābhisaṃbodhanatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 1 38.9]
anena āyuṣman śāriputra evaṃrūpeṇa manasikāreṇa icchāmi bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvaṃ viharantamanena vihāreṇeti | [ASāh, 1 38.10]
{ASāh, 2}
tena khalu punaḥ samayena śakro devānāmindrastasyāmeva parṣadi saṃnipatitaḥ saṃniṣaṇṇo 'bhūt catvāriṃśatā trayastriṃśatkāyikair devaputrasahasraiḥ sārdham | [ASāh, 2 1.1]
catvāraś ca lokapālā viṃśatyā cāturmahārājakāyikair devaputrasahasraiḥ sārdham | [ASāh, 2 1.2]
brahmāpi sahāpatirdaśabhir brahmakāyikair devaputrasahasraiḥ sārdham | [ASāh, 2 1.3]
pañca ca śuddhāvāsānāṃ devaputrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi tasyāmeva parṣadi saṃnipatitāni saṃniṣaṇṇānyabhūvan | [ASāh, 2 1.4]
yo 'pi ca devānāṃ svakarmavipākajo 'vabhāsaḥ so 'pi sarvo buddhānubhāvena buddhatejasā buddhādhiṣṭhānenābhibhūto 'bhūt | [ASāh, 2 1.5]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtiṃ sthavirametadavocat imānyārya subhūte saṃbahulāni devaputrasahasrāṇi asyāṃ parṣadi saṃnipatitāni saṃniṣaṇṇāni āryasya subhūterantikātprajñāpāramitāṃ śrotukāmāni bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām upadeśam avavādānuśāsanīṃ ca | [ASāh, 2 2.1]
tatkathaṃ bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthātavyam kathaṃ śikṣitavyam kathaṃ yogamāpattavyam sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha tena hi kauśika upadekṣyāmi te buddhānubhāvena buddhatejasā buddhādhiṣṭhānena | [ASāh, 2 2.2]
yairdevaputrairanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittaṃ notpāditam tairutpādayitavyam | [ASāh, 2 2.3]
ye tvavakrāntāḥ samyaktvaniyāmam na te bhavyā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittamutpādayitum | [ASāh, 2 2.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ baddhasīmāno hi te saṃsārasrotasaḥ | [ASāh, 2 2.5]
abhavyā hi te punaḥ punaḥ saṃsaraṇāya anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittamutpādayitum | [ASāh, 2 2.6]
api nu khalu punasteṣāmapyanumode | [ASāh, 2 2.7]
sacette 'pyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau cittānyutpādayeran nāhaṃ kuśalamūlasyāntarāyaṃ karomi | [ASāh, 2 2.8]
viśiṣṭebhyo hi dharmebhyo viśiṣṭatamā dharmā adhyālambitavyāḥ | [ASāh, 2 2.9]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimāmantrayate sma sādhu sādhu subhūte sādhu khalu punastvaṃ subhūte yastvaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmutsāhaṃ dadāsi | [ASāh, 2 3.1]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat kṛtajñairasmābhirbhagavan bhagavato bhavitavyaṃ nākṛtajñaiḥ | [ASāh, 2 3.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ paurvakāṇāṃ hi bhagavaṃstathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantike 'smadarthe bhagavān yathā brahmacaryaṃ bodhāya caran pūrvaṃ bodhisattvabhūta eva san yaiḥ śrāvakairavavadito 'nuśiṣṭaś ca pāramitāsu tatra bhagavatā caratā anuttaraṃ jñānamutpāditam | [ASāh, 2 3.3]
evaṃ bhagavan asmābhir api bodhisattvā mahāsattvā anuparigrahītavyā anuparivārayitavyāśca samparigrahītavyāḥ saṃparivārayitavyāś ca | [ASāh, 2 3.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ asmābhir api hi bhagavan bodhisattvā mahāsattvā anuparigṛhītā anuparivāritāśca samparigṛhītāḥ saṃparivāritāś ca kṣipramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyante | [ASāh, 2 3.5]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ śakraṃ devānāmindramāmantrayate sma tena hi kauśika śṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuru bhāṣiṣye 'haṃ te yathā bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.1]
śūnyatāyāṃ kauśika tiṣṭhatā bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.2]
tena hi kauśika bodhisattvena mahāsattvena mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddhena bhavitavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.3]
na rūpe sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.4]
na vedanāyāṃ na saṃjñāyāṃ na saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 2 4.5]
na vijñāne sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.6]
na cakṣuṣi sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.7]
na rūpe sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.8]
na cakṣurvijñāne sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.9]
na cakṣuḥsaṃsparśe sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.10]
na cakṣuḥsaṃsparśajāyāṃ vedanāyāṃ sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.11]
evaṃ na śrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaḥsu sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.12]
na śabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyadharmeṣu na śrotravijñāne yāvanna manovijñāne | [ASāh, 2 4.13]
na manaḥsaṃsparśe na manaḥsaṃsparśajāyāṃ vedanāyāṃ sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.14]
na pṛthivīdhātau sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.15]
nābdhātau na tejodhātau na vāyudhātau nākāśadhātau na vijñānadhātau sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.16]
na smṛtyupasthāneṣu sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.17]
na samyakprahāṇarddhipādendriyabalabodhyaṅgeṣu na mārgāṅgeṣu sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.18]
na srotaāpattiphale sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.19]
na sakṛdāgāmiphale na anāgāmiphale nārhattve sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.20]
na pratyekabuddhatve sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.21]
na buddhatve sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.22]
iti hi rūpamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.23]
iti hi vedaneti saṃjñeti saṃskārā iti | [ASāh, 2 4.24]
iti hi vijñānamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.25]
iti hi cakṣuriti yāvanmanaḥsaṃsparśajā vedaneti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.26]
iti hi pṛthivīdhāturiti yāvadvijñānadhāturiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.27]
iti hi smṛtyupasthānānīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.28]
iti hi samyakprahāṇarddhipādendriyabalabodhyaṅgānīti iti hi mārgāṅgānīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.29]
iti hi srotaāpattiphalamiti na sthātavyam iti hi sakṛdāgāmiphalamiti anāgāmiphalamiti arhattvamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.30]
iti hi pratyekabuddhatvamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.31]
iti hi buddhatvamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.32]
rūpaṃ nityamanityamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.33]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.34]
vijñānaṃ nityamanityamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.35]
rūpaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.36]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.37]
vijñānaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.38]
rūpaṃ śūnyam aśūnyam iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.39]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.40]
vijñānaṃ śūnyam aśūnyam iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.41]
rūpamātmānātmeti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.42]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.43]
vijñānamātmānātmeti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.44]
rūpaṃ śubhamaśubhamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.45]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.46]
vijñānaṃ śubhamaśubhamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.47]
rūpaṃ śūnyamupalabhyate veti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.48]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 4.49]
vijñānaṃ śūnyamupalabhyate veti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.50]
srotaāpattiphalamasaṃskṛtaprabhāvitamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.51]
evaṃ sakṛdāgāmiphalamanāgāmiphalamarhattvamasaṃskṛtaprabhāvitamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.52]
pratyekabuddhatvamasaṃskṛtaprabhāvitamiti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.53]
srotaāpanno dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.54]
srotaāpannāḥ saptakṛto bhavaparamā iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.55]
sakṛdāgāmī dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.56]
sakṛdāgāmyapariniṣṭhitatvāt sakṛd imaṃ lokam āgamya duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyatīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.57]
anāgāmī dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam anāgāmī anāgamya imaṃ lokaṃ tatraiva parinirvāsyatīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.58]
arhan dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.59]
arhannihaiva anupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāsyatīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.60]
pratyekabuddho dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.61]
pratyekabuddho 'tikramya śrāvakabhūmim aprāpya buddhabhūmiṃ parinirvāsyatīti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.62]
buddho dakṣiṇīya iti na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.63]
buddho 'tikramya pṛthagjanabhūmimatikramya śrāvakabhūmimatikramya pratyekabuddhabhūmim aprameyāṇām asaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmarthaṃ kṛtvā aprameyāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni sattvakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi parinirvāpya aprameyānasaṃkhyeyān sattvān śrāvakapratyekabuddhasamyaksaṃbuddhatvaniyatān kṛtvā buddhabhūmau sthitvā buddhakṛtyaṃ kṛtvā anupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau buddhaparinirvāṇena parinirvāsyati ityevamapyanena na sthātavyam | [ASāh, 2 4.64]
atha khalvāyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasyaitadabhavat yadi buddho 'tikramya pṛthagjanabhūmimatikramya śrāvakabhūmimatikramya pratyekabuddhabhūmimaprameyāṇāmasaṃkhyeyānāṃ sattvānāmarthaṃ kṛtvā aprameyāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni sattvakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi parinirvāpya aprameyānasaṃkhyeyān sattvān śrāvakapratyekabuddhasamyaksaṃbuddhatvaniyatān kṛtvā buddhabhūmau sthitvā buddhakṛtyaṃ kṛtvā anupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau buddhaparinirvāṇena parinirvāsyati ityevamapyanena na sthātavyam tatkathaṃ punaranena sthātavyaṃ kathaṃ śikṣitavyamiti atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena āyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasya cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat tatkiṃ manyase āyuṣman śāriputra kva tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sthitaḥ āyuṣmān śāriputra āha na kvacidāyuṣman subhūte tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sthitaḥ | [ASāh, 2 5.1]
tatkasya hetor apratiṣṭhitamānaso hi tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ | [ASāh, 2 5.2]
sa naiva saṃskṛte dhātau sthito nāpyasaṃskṛte dhātau sthito na ca tato vyutthitaḥ | [ASāh, 2 5.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evameva āyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena sthātavyam evaṃ śikṣitavyam yathā tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho na kvacitsthito nāsthito na viṣṭhito nāviṣṭhitaḥ tathā sthāsyāmītyevamanena śikṣitavyam | [ASāh, 2 6.1]
yathā tathāgatasthānaṃ tathā sthāsyāmīti tathā śikṣiṣye iti yathā tathāgatasthānaṃ tathā sthāsyāmīti tathā śikṣiṣye iti yathā tathāgatasthānaṃ tathā sthāsyāmīti susthito 'sthānayogeneti evamatra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena sthātavyamevaṃ śikṣitavyam | [ASāh, 2 6.2]
evaṃ hi śikṣamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo viharatyanena prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa avirahitaścānena manasikāreṇeti | [ASāh, 2 6.3]
atha khalu tatra parṣadi keṣāṃciddevaputrāṇāmetadabhūt yāni tāni yakṣāṇāṃ yakṣabhāṣitāni yakṣarutāni yakṣapadāni yakṣamantritāni yakṣapravyāhṛtāni tāni vijñāyante jalpyamānāni | [ASāh, 2 7.1]
na punaridaṃ vijñāyate yatsubhūtiḥ sthaviro bhāṣate pravyāharati deśayatyupadiśati | [ASāh, 2 7.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena teṣāṃ devaputrāṇāmimamevaṃrūpaṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya tān devaputrānāmantrayate sma na vijñāyate na vijñāyate idaṃ devaputrāḥ | [ASāh, 2 7.3]
tathā hi nātra kiṃcitsūcyate nātra kiṃcit śrūyate | [ASāh, 2 7.4]
atha khalu teṣāṃ devaputrāṇāṃ punarevaitadabhūt uttānīkariṣyati bata ayamāryasubhūtiḥ | [ASāh, 2 8.1]
uttānīkariṣyati batāyamāryasubhūtiriti | [ASāh, 2 8.2]
dūrāddūrataramāryasubhūtiḥ praviśati sūkṣmātsūkṣmataram | [ASāh, 2 8.3]
gambhīrād gambhīrataram āryasubhūtiḥ praviśati deśayati bhāṣata iti | [ASāh, 2 8.4]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena punar api teṣāmeva devaputrāṇāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya tān devaputrānāmantrayate sma tena hi devaputrāḥ yaḥ srotaāpattiphalaṃ prāptukāmaḥ srotaāpattiphale sthātukāmaḥ sa nemāṃ kṣāntim anāgamya peyālam | [ASāh, 2 8.5]
yaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphalaṃ prāptukāmaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphale sthātukāmaḥ yo 'nāgāmiphalaṃ prāptukāmo 'nāgāmiphale sthātukāmaḥ yo 'rhattvaṃ prāptukāmo 'rhattve sthātukāmaḥ yaḥ pratyekabodhiṃ prāptukāmaḥ pratyekabodhau sthātukāmaḥ sa nemāṃ kṣāntim anāgamya | [ASāh, 2 8.6]
yo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ prāptukāmo 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau sthātukāmaḥ sa nemāṃ kṣāntim anāgamya | [ASāh, 2 8.7]
atha khalu punar api teṣāṃ devaputrāṇāmetadabhavat kiṃrūpā asya āryasubhūter dhārmaśravaṇikā eṣṭavyāḥ atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbuddhānubhāvena teṣāṃ devaputrāṇāṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya tān devaputrānāmantrayate sma māyānirmitasadṛśā hi devaputrā mama dhārmaśravaṇikā eṣṭavyāḥ | [ASāh, 2 9.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi te naiva śroṣyanti na ca sākṣātkariṣyanti | [ASāh, 2 9.2]
atha khalu te devaputrā āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocan kiṃ punarārya subhūte māyopamāste sattvā na te māyā evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtistān devaputrānetadavocat māyopamāste devaputrāḥ sattvāḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.1]
svapnopamāste devaputrāḥ sattvāḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.2]
iti hi māyā ca sattvāś ca advayametad advaidhīkāram iti hi svapnaś ca sattvāś ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 2 10.3]
sarvadharmā api devaputrā māyopamāḥ svapnopamāḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.4]
srotaāpanno 'pi māyopamaḥ svapnopamaḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.5]
srotaāpattiphalam api māyopamaṃ svapnopamam | [ASāh, 2 10.6]
evaṃ sakṛdāgāmy api sakṛdāgāmiphalamapi anāgāmy api anāgāmiphalamapi arhann api arhattvam api māyopamaṃ svapnopamam | [ASāh, 2 10.7]
pratyekabuddho 'pi māyopamaḥ svapnopamaḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.8]
pratyekabuddhatvam api māyopamaṃ svapnopamam | [ASāh, 2 10.9]
samyaksaṃbuddho 'pi māyopamaḥ svapnopamaḥ | [ASāh, 2 10.10]
samyaksaṃbuddhatvam api māyopamaṃ svapnopamam | [ASāh, 2 10.11]
atha khalu devaputrā āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocan samyaksaṃbuddho 'pyārya subhūte māyopamaḥ svapnopama iti vadasi samyaksaṃbuddhatvam api māyopamaṃ svapnopamamiti vadasi subhūtirāha nirvāṇam api devaputrā māyopamaṃ svapnopamamiti vadāmi kiṃ punaranyaṃ dharmam | [ASāh, 2 10.12]
te devaputrā āhuḥ nirvāṇamapyārya subhūte māyopamaṃ svapnopamamiti vadasi āyuṣmān subhūtirāha tadyadi devaputrā nirvāṇādapyanyaḥ kaściddharmo viśiṣṭataraḥ syāt tamapyahaṃ māyopamaṃ svapnopamamiti vadeyam | [ASāh, 2 10.13]
iti hi devaputrā māyā ca nirvāṇaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 2 10.14]
iti hi svapnaś ca nirvāṇaṃ ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram | [ASāh, 2 10.15]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputraḥ āyuṣmāṃś ca pūrṇo maitrāyaṇīputraḥ āyuṣmāṃś ca mahākoṣṭhilaḥ āyuṣmāṃś ca mahākātyāyanaḥ āyuṣmāṃś ca mahākāśyapaḥ anye ca mahāśrāvakā anekairbodhisattvasahasraiḥ sārdhamāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtiṃ sthaviramāmantrayante sma ke 'syā āyuṣman subhūte prajñāpāramitāyā evaṃ nirdiśyamānāyāḥ pratyeṣakā bhaviṣyanti atha khalvāyuṣmānānandastān sthavirānetadavocat te khalvāyuṣmanto veditavyā avinivartanīyā bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ dṛṣṭisampannā vā pudgalāḥ arhanto vā kṣīṇāsravāḥ ye 'syāḥ prajñāpāramitāyā evaṃ nirdiśyamānāyāḥ pratyeṣakā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 2 11.1]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ sthavirastān sthavirānetadavocat nāsyā āyuṣmantaḥ prajñāpāramitāyā evaṃ nirdiśyamānāyāḥ kecitpratyeṣakā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 2 12.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi atra na kaściddharmaḥ sūcyate na kaściddharmaḥ paridīpyate na kaściddharmaḥ prajñapyate | [ASāh, 2 12.2]
tadyathaivātra na kaściddharmaḥ sūcyate na kaściddharmaḥ paridīpyate na kaściddharmaḥ prajñapyate tathaivāsyāḥ prajñāpāramitāyā evaṃ nirdiśyamānāyā na kaścitpratyeṣako bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 2 12.3]
atha khalu śakrasya devānāmindrasyaitadabhūt asya dharmaparyāyasya āryeṇa subhūtinā bhāṣyamāṇasya pūjārthaṃ yannvahaṃ puṣpāṇyabhinirmāya āryaṃ subhūtimabhyavakireyamiti | [ASāh, 2 13.1]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindrastasyāṃ velāyāṃ puṣpāṇyabhinirmāya āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimabhyavākirat | [ASāh, 2 13.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmataḥ subhūteḥ sthavirasya śakraṃ devānāmindramanuvyāharaṇāyaitadabhūt na khalu punarimāni puṣpāṇi mayā trāyastriṃśeṣu deveṣu pracaranti dṛṣṭapūrvāṇi yānīmāni śakreṇa devānāmindreṇa abhyavakīrṇāni | [ASāh, 2 13.3]
nirmitānyetāni puṣpāṇi | [ASāh, 2 13.4]
naitāni puṣpāṇi vṛkṣagulmalatānirjātāni yāni śakreṇa devānāmindreṇābhyavakīrṇāni manomayānyetāni puṣpāṇīti | [ASāh, 2 13.5]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmataḥ subhūteścetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat anirjātānyetānyārya subhūte puṣpāṇi | [ASāh, 2 13.6]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi manonirjātāni kānicitpuṣpāṇi nāpi vṛkṣagulmalatānirjātāni | [ASāh, 2 13.7]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat yattvaṃ kauśika evaṃ vadasi anirjātānyetāni puṣpāṇi naitāni manonirjātāni nāpi vṛkṣagulmalatānirjātānīti | [ASāh, 2 13.8]
yatkauśika anirjātaṃ na tatpuṣpam | [ASāh, 2 13.9]
atha khalu śakrasya devānāmindrasyaitadabhūt gambhīraprajño batāyamāryaḥ subhūtiḥ | [ASāh, 2 13.10]
tāṃ ca nāma padaprajñaptiṃ nirdiśati tāṃ ca na virodhayati tāṃ cottānīkaroti tāmeva copadiśati | [ASāh, 2 13.11]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmataṃ subhūtimetadavocat evametadārya subhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 2 13.12]
evaṃ cātra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena śikṣitavyaṃ yathā āryasubhūtirupadiśati | [ASāh, 2 13.13]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat evametatkauśika evam etat | [ASāh, 2 13.14]
evamatra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena śikṣitavyam | [ASāh, 2 13.15]
evaṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na srotaāpattiphale śikṣate na sakṛdāgāmiphale na anāgāmiphale nārhattve śikṣate na pratyekabuddhatve śikṣate na buddhatve śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 13.16]
yo nāsu bhūmiṣu śikṣate sa buddhatve sarvajñatve vā śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 13.17]
yo buddhatve sarvajñatve vā śikṣate so 'prameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu buddhadharmeṣu śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 13.18]
yo 'prameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu buddhadharmeṣu śikṣate sa na rūpasya vivṛddhaye śikṣate na parihāṇāya | [ASāh, 2 13.19]
evaṃ sa na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 2 13.20]
sa na vijñānasya vivṛddhaye śikṣate na parihāṇāya | [ASāh, 2 13.21]
yo na rūpasya vivṛddhaye śikṣate na parihāṇāya | [ASāh, 2 13.22]
evaṃ na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 2 13.23]
yo na vijñānasya vivṛddhaye śikṣate na parihāṇāya sa na rūpasya parigrahāya śikṣate notsargāya | [ASāh, 2 13.24]
evaṃ sa na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 2 13.25]
sa na vijñānasya parigrahāya śikṣate notsargāya nāpi kasyaciddharmasya parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 13.26]
yo na kasyaciddharmasya parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate sa na sarvajñatāyā api parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 13.27]
evaṃ śikṣamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣate sarvajñatāyāṃ niryāsyati | [ASāh, 2 13.28]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat ya āyuṣman subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na kasyaciddharmasya parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate sa na sarvajñatāyā api parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 14.1]
evaṃ śikṣamāṇa āyuṣmān subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣate sarvajñatāyāṃ niryāsyati | [ASāh, 2 14.2]
āyuṣmān subhūtirāha evametadāyuṣman śāriputra evam etat | [ASāh, 2 15.1]
ya āyuṣman śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na kasyaciddharmasya parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate sa na sarvajñatāyā api parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 15.2]
sarvabuddhadharmāṇām api na parigrahāya śikṣate notpādāya nāntardhānāya śikṣate | [ASāh, 2 15.3]
evaṃ cāyuṣman śāriputra śikṣamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvajñatāyāṃ śikṣate sarvajñatāyāṃ niryāsyati | [ASāh, 2 15.4]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat prajñāpāramitā ārya śāriputra bodhisattvena mahāsattvena kuto gaveṣitavyāḥ śāriputra āha prajñāpāramitā kauśika bodhisattvena mahāsattvena āyuṣmataḥ subhūteḥ parivartād gaveṣitavyā | [ASāh, 2 16.1]
evamukte śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat kasyaiṣa ārya śāriputra anubhāvo veditavyaḥ kasyaitadadhiṣṭhānaṃ veditavyaṃ yadāryasubhūtiḥ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣate āyuṣmān śāriputra āha tathāgatasyaiṣa kauśika anubhāvo veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 2 16.2]
tathāgatasyaitadadhiṣṭhānaṃ veditavyaṃ yadāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣate | [ASāh, 2 16.3]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat yatkauśika evaṃ vadasi kasyaiṣo 'nubhāvo veditavyaḥ kasyaitadanuṣṭhānaṃ veditavyaṃ yadāryasubhūtiḥ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣate iti tathāgatasyaiṣa kauśika anubhāvo veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 2 16.4]
tathāgatasyaitadadhiṣṭhānaṃ veditavyaṃ yadahaṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣe | [ASāh, 2 16.5]
yad api kauśika evaṃ vadasi prajñāpāramitā bodhisattvena mahāsattvena kuto gaveṣitavyeti prajñāpāramitā kauśika bodhisattvena mahāsattvena na rūpādgaveṣitavyā nāpyanyatra rūpād gaveṣitavyā | [ASāh, 2 16.6]
evaṃ na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārebhyaḥ na vijñānād gaveṣitavyāḥ nāpyanyatra vijñānād gaveṣitavyā | [ASāh, 2 16.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi na rūpaṃ prajñāpāramitā nāpyanyatra rūpātprajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 16.8]
evaṃ na vedanā na saṃjñā na saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 16.9]
na vijñānaṃ prajñāpāramitā nāpyanyatra vijñānātprajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 16.10]
evamukte śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat mahāpāramiteyamārya subhūte yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.1]
apramāṇapāramiteyamārya subhūte yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.2]
aparimāṇapāramiteyamārya subhūte yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.3]
anantapāramiteyamārya subhūte yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.4]
sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha evametatkauśika evam etat | [ASāh, 2 17.5]
mahāpāramiteyaṃ kauśika yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.6]
apramāṇapāramiteyaṃ kauśika yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.7]
aparimāṇapāramiteyaṃ kauśika yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.8]
anantapāramiteyaṃ kauśika yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.9]
tatkasya hetoḥ rūpamahattayā hi kauśika mahāpāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.10]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 17.11]
vijñānamahattayā hi kauśika mahāpāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.12]
rūpāpramāṇatayā kauśika apramāṇapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.13]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 17.14]
vijñānāpramāṇatayā kauśika apramāṇapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.15]
rūpāparimāṇatayā kauśika aparimāṇapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.16]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 17.17]
vijñānāparimāṇatayā kauśika aparimāṇapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.18]
rūpānantatayā kauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.19]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 2 17.20]
vijñānānantatayā kauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.21]
evaṃ mahāpāramiteti kauśika nābhiniviśate | [ASāh, 2 17.22]
evamapramāṇapāramiteti evamaparimāṇapāramiteti evamanantapāramiteti nābhiniviśate | [ASāh, 2 17.23]
tasmātkauśika mahāpāramiteyam apramāṇapāramiteyam aparimāṇapāramiteyam anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 17.24]
ārambaṇānantatayā kauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.1]
sattvānantatayā kauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.2]
kathaṃ punaḥ kauśika ārambaṇānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā sarvadharmāṇāṃ hi kauśika yato nānto na madhyaṃ na paryavasānamupalabhyate tataḥ kauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.3]
anena kauśika paryāyeṇa ārambaṇānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.4]
punaraparaṃ kauśika yasmātsarvadharmā anantā aparyantāḥ na teṣāmanto vā madhyaṃ vā paryavasānaṃ vā upalabhyate tasmātkauśika anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.5]
tatkasya hetoḥ rūpasya hi kauśika nānto na madhyaṃ na paryavasānamupalabhyate | [ASāh, 2 18.6]
evaṃ vedanāyāḥ saṃjñāyāḥ saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 2 18.7]
vijñānasya hi kauśika nānto na madhyaṃ na paryavasānamupalabhyate | [ASāh, 2 18.8]
anenāpi kauśika paryāyeṇa ārambaṇānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 18.9]
punaraparaṃ kauśika sattvo 'nanto 'paryantaḥ | [ASāh, 2 19.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi sattvasyānto vā madhyaṃ vā paryavasānaṃ vopalabhyate | [ASāh, 2 19.2]
tasmātkauśika sattvānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 19.3]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat kathamāyuṣman subhūte sattvānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha na hi kauśika gaṇanāyogena vā gaṇanābahutvena vā sattvānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 19.4]
śakra āha kathaṃ tarhīdānīmārya subhūte sattvānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha tatkaṃ manyase kauśika katamasyaitaddharmasyādhivacanaṃ yaduta sattvaḥ sattva iti śakra āha naitadārya subhūte dharmasyādhivacanaṃ na adharmādhivacanaṃ yaduta sattvaḥ sattva iti | [ASāh, 2 20.1]
āgantukametannāmadheyaṃ prakṣiptam | [ASāh, 2 20.2]
avastukametannāmadheyaṃ prakṣiptam | [ASāh, 2 20.3]
anātmīyam etannāmadheyaṃ prakṣiptam | [ASāh, 2 20.4]
anārambaṇametannāmadheyaṃ prakṣiptaṃ yaduta sattvaḥ sattva iti | [ASāh, 2 20.5]
sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha tatkiṃ manyase kauśika kācidatra sattvaparidīpanā kṛtā śakra āha no hīdamārya subhūte | [ASāh, 2 20.6]
subhūtirāha yatra kauśika na kācitsattvaparidīpanā kṛtā tatra kā sattvānantatā sacetkauśika tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho 'nantavijñaptighoṣeṇa gambhīranirghoṣeṇa svareṇa gaṅgānadīvālukopamān kalpān api vitiṣṭhamānaḥ sattvaḥ sattva iti vācaṃ bhāṣeta api nu tatra kaścitsattva utpanno va utpatsyate vā utpadyate vā niruddho vā nirotsyate vā nirudhyate vā śakra āha no hīdamārya subhūte | [ASāh, 2 20.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ ādiśuddhatvādādipariśuddhatvātsattvasya | [ASāh, 2 20.8]
subhūtirāha anenāpi kauśika paryāyeṇa evaṃ sattvānantatayā anantapāramiteyaṃ yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 2 20.9]
evaṃ ca punaḥ kauśika sattvānantatayā prajñāpāramitānantatā veditavyā | [ASāh, 2 20.10]
atha khalu sendrakā devāḥ sabrahmakāḥ saprajāpatikāḥ sarṣinaranārīgaṇās trirudānam udānayanti sma aho dharmaḥ aho dharmaḥ aho dharmasya dharmatā | [ASāh, 2 21.1]
yastathāgatasya prādurbhāvaḥ sa āryeṇa subhūtinā sthavireṇa subhāṣiteneha sūcyate deśyate prakāśyate prabhāvyate | [ASāh, 2 21.2]
tathāgataṃ taṃ vayaṃ bhagavan bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamadyāgreṇa dhārayiṣyāmo yo 'nayā prajñāpāramitayā avirahito bhaviṣyati yo 'pi ca anena bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāvihāreṇa vihariṣyati | [ASāh, 2 21.3]
atha khalu bhagavāṃstān sendrakān sabrahmakān saprajāpatikān sarṣinaranārīgaṇānāmantrayate sma evametaddevaputrāḥ evam etat | [ASāh, 2 22.1]
yadāhaṃ devaputrā dīpaṃkarasya tathāgatasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyāntike dīpavatyāṃ rājadhānyām antarāyaṇamadhyagato 'nayā prajñāpāramitayā avirahito 'bhūvam tadāhaṃ dīpaṃkareṇa tathāgatenārhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhena vyākṛto 'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ māṇava anāgate 'dhvani asaṃkhyeyaiḥ kalpaiḥ śākyamunirnāma tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho vidyācaraṇasampannaḥ sugato lokavidanuttaraḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ śāstā devānāṃ ca manuṣyānāṃ ca buddho bhagavāniti | [ASāh, 2 22.2]
atha khalu te devaputrā bhagavantametadavocan āścaryaṃ bhagavan paramāścaryaṃ sugata | [ASāh, 2 22.3]
yāvadiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ sarvajñatāyā āhārikā anuparigrāhikā ceti | [ASāh, 2 22.4]
{ASāh, 3}
atha khalu bhagavān ye tatra devaputrāḥ parṣadi saṃnipatitāḥ saṃniṣaṇṇāścābhūvan yāś ca bhikṣubhikṣuṇyupāsakopāsikāḥ saṃnipatitāḥ saṃniṣaṇṇāścābhūvan tān devaputrān saṃnipatitān saṃniṣaṇṇāṃś ca viditvā tāś ca sarvāścatasraḥ parṣadaḥ saṃnipatitāḥ saṃniṣaṇṇāś ca viditvā kāmāvacarān rūpāvacarāṃś ca devaputrān brahmakāyikāṃś ca devaputrān ābhāsvarāṃś ca parīttaśubhāṃś ca akaniṣṭhāṃś ca devaputrān sākṣiṇaḥ sthāpayitvā śakradevendrapramukhān kāmāvacarān devaputrān mahābrahmapramukhāṃś ca brahmakāyikān devaputrānābhāsvarāṃś ca devaputrānāmantrayate sma yo hi kaściddevaputrāḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati na tasya māro vā mārakāyikā vā devatā avatāraprekṣiṇyo 'vatāragaveṣiṇyo 'vatāraṃ lapsyante | [ASāh, 3 1.1]
nāpi tasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā manuṣyā vā amanuṣyā vā avatāraprekṣiṇo 'vatāragaveṣiṇo 'vatāraṃ lapsyante | [ASāh, 3 1.2]
nāpi sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā viṣamāparihāreṇa kālaṃ kariṣyati | [ASāh, 3 1.3]
punaraparaṃ devaputrāḥ ye devaputrā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau samprasthitāḥ yaiś ca devaputrairiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā nodgṛhītā na dhāritā na vācitā na paryavāptā na pravartitā te devaputrāstaṃ kulaputraṃ vā kuladuhitaraṃ vā upasaṃkramitavyaṃ maṃsyante tasya ca kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇato dhārayato vācayataḥ paryavāpnuvataḥ pravartayamānasyāntikācchroṣyanti śrutvā codgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti | [ASāh, 3 2.1]
na ca khalu punardevaputrāstasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇato dhārayato vācayataḥ paryavāpnuvataḥ pravartayamānasya araṇyagatasya vā vṛkṣamūlagatasya vā śūnyāgāragatasya vā abhyavakāśagatasya vā pathi gatasya vā utpathagatasya vā aṭavīgatasya vā mahāsamudragatasya vā tatra tatropasaṃkrāmato vā caṅkramyamāṇasya vā sthitasya vā niṣaṇṇasya vā vipannasya vā bhayaṃ vā bhaviṣyati stambhitatvaṃ vā bhaviṣyati utpatsyate vā | [ASāh, 3 2.2]
atha khalu catvāro mahārājāno bhagavantametadavocan āścaryaṃ bhagavan yadimāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇan dhārayan vācayan paryavāpnuvan pravartayan sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā yānatraye sattvān vinayati na ca sattvasaṃjñāmutpādayati | [ASāh, 3 3.1]
vayaṃ bhagavaṃstasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhāsyāmaḥ ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati | [ASāh, 3 3.2]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat aham api bhagavaṃstasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhāsyāmi ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati | [ASāh, 3 4.1]
brahmāpi sahāpatiḥ sārdhaṃ brahmakāyikair devaputrair bhagavantametadavocat aham api bhagavaṃstasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhāsyāmi ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati | [ASāh, 3 5.1]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yadimāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇan dhārayan vācayan paryavāpnuvan pravartayan sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imān yato dṛṣṭadhārmikān guṇān pratilabhate parigṛhṇāti kiṃ punarbhagavan prajñāpāramitāyām udgṛhītāyāṃ sarvāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitā udgṛhītā bhavanti evamukte bhagavān śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat evametatkauśika evam etat | [ASāh, 3 6.1]
prajñāpāramitāyāṃ kauśika udgṛhītāyāṃ sarvāḥ ṣaṭ pāramitā udgṛhītā bhavanti | [ASāh, 3 6.2]
punaraparaṃ kauśika prajñāpāramitāyām udgṛhītāyāṃ dhāritāyāṃ vācitāyāṃ paryavāptāyāṃ pravartitāyāṃ sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā dṛṣṭadhārmikān guṇān parigṛhṇāti | [ASāh, 3 6.3]
tān kauśika sarvān śṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuru bhāṣiṣye 'haṃ te | [ASāh, 3 6.4]
sādhu bhagavanniti śakro devānāmindro bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [ASāh, 3 6.5]
bhagavānetadavocat tatra kauśika ye mama dharmaṃ vigrahītavyaṃ maṃsyante vivaditavyaṃ maṃsyante virodhayitavyaṃ maṃsyante teṣāṃ vigrahītukāmānāṃ vivaditukāmānāṃ virodhayitukāmānām utpannotpannā vigrahā vivādā virodhāḥ punarevāntardhāsyanti na sthāsyanti | [ASāh, 3 6.6]
teṣāṃ vigrahītukāmānāṃ vivaditukāmānāṃ virodhayitukāmānāṃ na te 'bhiprāyāḥ paripūriṃ gamiṣyanti | [ASāh, 3 6.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ evaṃ hyetatkauśika bhavati ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā udgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati tasyaivaṃ tānyutpannotpannānyadhikaraṇāni punarevāntardhāsyanti na sthāsyanti | [ASāh, 3 6.8]
teṣāṃ vigrahītukāmānāṃ vivaditukāmānāṃ virodhayitukāmānāṃ na te 'bhiprāyāḥ paripūriṃ gamiṣyanti | [ASāh, 3 6.9]
imam api sa kauśika kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā dṛṣṭadhārmikaṃ guṇaṃ parigṛhṇāti ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇāti dhārayati vācayati paryavāpnoti pravartayati deśayati upadiśati uddiśati svādhyāyati | [ASāh, 3 6.10]
tadyathāpi nāma kauśika maghī nāmauṣadhī sarvaviṣapraśamanī | [ASāh, 3 6.11]
tatra āśīviṣeṇa jantunā bubhukṣitena āhārārthinā āhāragaveṣiṇā kaścideva prāṇakajāto janturdṛṣṭo bhavet | [ASāh, 3 6.12]
sa āśīviṣastaṃ prāṇakajātaṃ gandhenānubadhnīyād anugacched āhārahetorbhakṣayitukāmaḥ | [ASāh, 3 6.13]
atha sa prāṇakajāto yena sā maghī nāmauṣadhī tenopasaṃkramet tenopasaṃkramya tiṣṭhet | [ASāh, 3 6.14]
atha sa āśīviṣastasyā oṣadhyā gandhenaiva pratyudāvarteta | [ASāh, 3 6.15]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi tasyā oṣadhyā bhaiṣajyaguṇaḥ sa tādṛśo yastasyāśīviṣasya tadviṣamabhibhavati | [ASāh, 3 6.16]
evaṃ balavatī hi sā oṣadhī | [ASāh, 3 6.17]
evameva kauśika yaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā va imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati tasya kauśika yāni tānyutpannotpannānyadhikaraṇāni vigrahā vivādā virodhā bhaviṣyanti te prajñāpāramitāyāstejasā balena sthāmataḥ prajñāpāramitābalādhānena kṣipraṃ tata evoparaṃsyanti upaśamiṣyanti antardhāsyanti na vivardhiṣyante | [ASāh, 3 6.18]
yato yata evotpatsyante tatra tatraiva nirotsyante antardhāsyanti na vivardhiṣyante na sthāsyanti | [ASāh, 3 6.19]
tatkasya hetoḥ prajñāpāramitā hi rāgādīnāṃ yāvannirvāṇagrāhasyopaśamayitrī na vivardhiketi | [ASāh, 3 6.20]
catvāraś ca tasya mahārājānaḥ śakraś ca devānāmindro brahmā ca sahāpatiḥ sarve ca buddhā bhagavanto bodhisattvāś ca rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhāsyanti ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati | [ASāh, 3 6.21]
ayaṃ tena kulaputreṇa vā kuladuhitā vā dṛṣṭadhārmiko guṇaḥ parigṛhīto bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 3 6.22]
punaraparaṃ kauśika yaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati sa ādeyavacanaś ca bhaviṣyati mṛduvacanaś ca bhaviṣyati mitavacanaś ca bhaviṣyati aprakīrṇavacanaś ca bhaviṣyati na ca krodhābhibhūto bhaviṣyati na ca mānābhibhūto bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 3 7.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi taṃ prajñāpāramitā paridamayati prajñāpāramitā pariṇamayati na krodhaṃ vardhayati na mānaṃ vardhayati | [ASāh, 3 7.2]
sa nopanāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti na vyāpādaṃ parigṛhṇāti nānuśayaṃ dhārayati | [ASāh, 3 7.3]
evaṃ carato 'sya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā smṛtirmaitrī cotpadyate | [ASāh, 3 7.4]
tasyaivaṃ bhavati sacedahaṃ vyāpādamutpādayiṣyāmi tenendriyāṇi me paribhetsyante mukhavarṇaś ca me dhakṣyate | [ASāh, 3 7.5]
ayuktaṃ caitanmama yadahamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau samprasthitaḥ tatra śikṣitukāmaḥ krodhasya vaśaṃ gaccheyam | [ASāh, 3 7.6]
ityevaṃ sa kṣiprameva smṛtiṃ pratilabhate | [ASāh, 3 7.7]
imam api sa kauśika kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā dṛṣṭadhārmikaṃ guṇaṃ parigṛhṇāti ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati | [ASāh, 3 7.8]
evamukte śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yatheyaṃ prajñāpāramitā paridamanāya pratyupasthitā anunāmāya bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānām | [ASāh, 3 7.9]
bhagavānāha punaraparaṃ kauśika ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā udgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyati upadekṣyati uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati sacetkulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmevamudgṛhṇan dhārayan vācayan paryavāpnuvan pravartayan deśayan upadiśayan uddiśan svādhyāyan saṃgrāme vartamāne saṃgrāmaśirasi samārūḍhaḥ syāt | [ASāh, 3 8.1]
tasya saṃgrāmamavatarato vā avatīrṇasya vā atikrāmato vā saṃgrāmamadhyagatasya vā tiṣṭhato vā niṣaṇṇasya vā asthānametatkauśika anavakāśo yattasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ manasi kurvato vā udgṛhṇato vā dhārayato vā vācayato vā paryavāpnuvato vā pravartayato vā deśayato vā upadiśato vā uddiśato vā svādhyāyato vā jīvitāntarāyo vā bhavet | [ASāh, 3 8.2]
paropakrameṇa jīvitāntarāyaṃ so 'nuprāpnuyāt naitatsthānaṃ vidyate | [ASāh, 3 8.3]
sacetpunastasya kaścitkauśika tatra śastraṃ vā daṇḍaṃ vā loṣṭaṃ vā anyadvā kṣipet naitattasya śarīre nipatet | [ASāh, 3 8.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ mahāvidyeyaṃ kauśika yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.5]
apramāṇeyaṃ kauśika vidyā yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.6]
aparimāṇeyaṃ kauśika vidyā yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.7]
anuttareyaṃ kauśika vidyā yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.8]
asameyaṃ kauśika vidyā yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.9]
asamasameyaṃ kauśika vidyā yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 3 8.10]
tatkasya hetoḥ atra hi kauśika vidyāyāṃ śikṣamāṇaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā nātmavyābādhāya cetayate na paravyābādhāya cetayate nobhayavyābādhāya cetayate | [ASāh, 3 8.11]
atra hi kauśika vidyāyāṃ śikṣamāṇo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbhotsyate sarvajñajñānaṃ ca pratilapsyate | [ASāh, 3 8.12]
tena so 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya sarvasattvānāṃ cittāni vyavalokayiṣyati | [ASāh, 3 8.13]
tatkasya hetoḥ atra hi kauśika vidyāyāṃ śikṣamāṇasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya na tatkiṃcidasti yanna prāptaṃ vā na jñātaṃ vā na sākṣātkṛtaṃ vā syāt | [ASāh, 3 8.14]
tasmātsarvajñajñānamityucyate | [ASāh, 3 8.15]
