sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha kiyacciracaritāvī sa bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyo ya iha gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpatsyate bhagavānāha vibhajya vyākaraṇīyametatsubhūte bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmindriyādhimātratayā | [ASāh, 7 10.1]
syātkhalu punaḥ subhūte paryāyo yena paryāyeṇa bodhisattvā bahūni buddhaśatāni bahūni buddhasahasrāṇi bahūni buddhaśatasahasrāṇi dṛṣṭvā teṣāmantike brahmacaryaṃ caritvā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ na śraddadhyurnādhimuñceyuḥ | [ASāh, 7 10.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ pūrvam api teṣāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāmantikādasyāṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyām agauravatā abhūt | [ASāh, 7 10.3]
agauravatayā aśuśrūṣaṇatā aśuśrūṣaṇatayā aparyupāsanatā aparyupāsanatayā aparipṛcchanatā aparipṛcchanatayā aśraddadhānatā aśraddadhānatayā tataḥ parṣaddhyo 'pakrāntāḥ te tatonidānaṃ dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyena karmaṇā kṛtena saṃcitena ācitena upacitena etarhy api gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyām apakrāmanti | [ASāh, 7 10.4]
agauravatayā aśraddadhānā anadhimuñcanto na kāyena na cittena sāmagrīṃ dadati | [ASāh, 7 10.5]
te sāmagrīm adadānā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ na jānanti na paśyanti na budhyante na vedayante | [ASāh, 7 10.6]
evaṃ te prajñāpāramitāṃ na śraddadhati | [ASāh, 7 10.7]
aśraddadhānā na śṛṇvanti | [ASāh, 7 10.8]
aśṛṇvanto na jānanti | [ASāh, 7 10.9]
ajānanto na paśyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.10]
apaśyanto na budhyante | [ASāh, 7 10.11]
abudhyamānā dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyaṃ karma kurvanti saṃcinvanti ācinvanti upacinvanti | [ASāh, 7 10.12]
te tena dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyena karmaṇā kṛtena saṃcitena ācitena upacitena duṣprajñasaṃvartanīyaṃ karmābhisaṃskariṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.13]
tena te duṣprajñasaṃvartanīyena karmaṇā abhisaṃskṛtena saṃcitenācitenopacitena imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāṃ deśyamānāmupadiśyamānāṃ pratyākhyāsyanti pratikṣepsyanti pratikrokṣyanti pratikṣipya ca apakramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.14]
asyāḥ khalu punaḥ subhūte prajñāpāramitāyāḥ pratyākhyānena pratikṣepeṇa pratikrośena atītānāgatapratyutpannānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ sarvajñatā pratyākhyātā bhavati pratikṣiptā bhavati pratikruṣṭā bhavati | [ASāh, 7 10.15]
te svasaṃtānānupahatya dagdhāḥ pareṣām apyalpabuddhikānām alpaprajñānām alpapuṇyānām alpakuśalamūlānāṃ pudgalānāṃ śraddhāmātrakasamanvāgatānāṃ premamātrakasamanvāgatānāṃ prasādamātrakasamanvāgatānāṃ chandamātrakasamanvāgatānām ādikarmikāṇām abhavyarūpāṇāṃ tad api śraddhāmātrakaṃ premamātrakaṃ prasādamātrakaṃ chandamātrakaṃ vicchandayiṣyanti vivecayiṣyanti vivartayiṣyanti nātra śikṣitavyamiti vakṣyanti naitadbuddhavacanamiti vācaṃ bhāṣiṣyante | [ASāh, 7 10.16]
evaṃ te ātmasaṃtānānupahatya vivecya parasaṃtānānapyupahatya vivecya prajñāpāramitāmabhyākhyāsyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.17]
prajñāpāramitāyām abhyākhyātāyāṃ sarvajñatā abhyākhyātā bhavati | [ASāh, 7 10.18]
sarvajñatāyām abhyākhyātāyām atītānāgatapratyutpannā buddhā bhagavanto 'bhyākhyātā bhavanti | [ASāh, 7 10.19]
te buddhānāṃ bhagavatāmantikādapakrāntā bhaviṣyanti dharmātparimuktā bhaviṣyanti saṃghāt paribāhyā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.20]
evaṃ teṣāṃ sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ triratnāt paribāhyabhāvo bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 10.21]
te sattvānāṃ hitasukhopacchedakriyayā mahānirayavipākasaṃvartanīyaṃ karma upaceṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.22]
te anenaivaṃrūpeṇa karmābhisaṃskāreṇopasthāpitena samutthāpitena dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyena duṣprajñasaṃvartanīyena karmaṇā bahūni varṣaśatāni bahūni varṣasahasrāṇi bahūni varṣaśatasahasrāṇi bahūni varṣakoṭīśatāni bahūni varṣakoṭīsahasrāṇi bahūni varṣakoṭīśatasahasrāṇi bahūni varṣakoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi mahānirayeṣūpapatsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.23]
te mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.24]
teṣāṃ tathā suciraṃ mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkrāmatāṃ tejaḥsaṃvartanī prādurbhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 10.25]
tejaḥsaṃvartanyāṃ prādurbhūtāyāṃ ye 'nyeṣu lokadhātuṣu mahānirayāḥ tatra te kṣepsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.26]
te teṣu mahānirayeṣu upapatsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.27]
te tatra vikṣiptāsteṣu mahānirayeṣūpapannāḥ samānāstatrāpi mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.28]
teṣāṃ tatrāpi mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkrāmatāṃ tatrāpi punareva tathaiva tejaḥsaṃvartanī prādurbhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 10.29]
te tasyāṃ tejaḥsaṃvartanyāṃ prādurbhūtāyāṃ tataścyutāḥ samānāḥ punareva anyeṣu lokadhātuṣu ye mahānirayāstatra kṣepsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.30]
te teṣu mahānirayeṣūpapatsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.31]
te tatrāpi tathaiva mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.32]
teṣāṃ tatrāpi suciraṃ mahānirayānmahānirayaṃ saṃkrāmatāṃ tatrāpi tathaiva tejaḥsaṃvartanī prādurbhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 10.33]
te tasyāṃ tejaḥsaṃvartanyāṃ prādurbhūtāyāṃ punareva tataścyutāstenaiva akṣīṇena sāvaśeṣeṇa karmaṇā ihaiva lokadhātau punaḥ kṣepsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.34]
kṣiptāḥ santo mahānirayeṣūpapatsyante | [ASāh, 7 10.35]
te punareva tāni mahānirayeṣu mahānti mahānirayaduḥkhāni pratyanubhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.36]
tāvatpratyanubhaviṣyanti yāvatpunareva tejaḥsaṃvartanī prādurbhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 10.37]
evaṃ te bahuduḥkhavedanīyaṃ karma pratyanubhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 10.38]
tatkasya hetoḥ yathāpi nāma durbhāṣitatvādvācaḥ | [ASāh, 7 10.39]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat pañca bhagavan ānantaryāṇi karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitāni asya manoduścaritasya vāgduścaritasya ca na prativarṇikāny api na anurūpāṇy api na pratirūpāṇy api bhavanti | [ASāh, 7 11.1]
bhagavānāha evametacchāriputra evam etat | [ASāh, 7 11.2]
pañcānantaryāṇi śāriputra karmāṇi kṛtānyupacitānyasya manoduścaritasya ca vāgduścaritasya ca na prativarṇikānyapi na anurūpāṇy api na pratirūpāṇy api asya karmaṇaḥ kṛtasya saṃcitasya ācitasya upacitasya | [ASāh, 7 11.3]
ye kecidimāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāṃ deśyamānām upadiśyamānāmuddiśyamānāṃ pratibādhitavyāṃ maṃsyante pratikṣepsyanti pratikrokṣyanti nātra śikṣitavyamiti vakṣyanti neyaṃ tathāgatabhāṣiteti vācaṃ bhāṣiṣyante tato 'nyān api sattvān vivecayiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 11.4]
te svasaṃtānānupahatya parasaṃtānānupahaniṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 11.5]
te svasaṃtānān saviṣān kṛtvā parasaṃtānān saviṣān kariṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 11.6]
svayaṃ naṣṭāḥ parān api nāśayiṣyanti | [ASāh, 7 11.7]
svayaṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitām ajānānā anavabudhyamānāḥ parān api grāhayiṣyanti nātra śikṣitavyamiti vācaṃ bhāṣiṣyante | [ASāh, 7 11.8]
nāhaṃ śāriputra evaṃrūpāṇāṃ pudgalānāṃ darśanamapyabhyanujānāmi kutastaiḥ saha saṃvāsaṃ kuto vā lābhasatkāraṃ kutaḥ sthānam tatkasya hetoḥ dharmadūṣakā hi te śāriputra tathārūpāḥ pudgalā veditavyā iti | [ASāh, 7 11.9]
kasambakajātāste śāriputra tathārūpāḥ pudgalā veditavyāḥ | [ASāh, 7 11.10]
kṛṣṇānirjātikāḥ kṛṣṇāhijātikāste śāriputra tathārūpāḥ pudgalā veditavyāḥ | [ASāh, 7 11.11]
teṣāṃ śāriputra tathārūpāṇāṃ pudgalānāṃ ye śrotavyaṃ maṃsyante sarve te anayena vyasanamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 7 11.12]
ye ca śāriputra prajñāpāramitāṃ dūṣayanti ime te śāriputra dharmadūṣakāḥ pudgalā veditavyāḥ | [ASāh, 7 11.13]
śāriputra āha na bhagavatā tasya pudgalasya tatropapannasya mahānirayagatasyātmabhāvasya pramāṇamākhyātam | [ASāh, 7 11.14]
bhagavānāha tiṣṭhatu śāriputra tasya pudgalasya tatropapannasya mahānirayagatasyātmabhāvasya pramāṇam | [ASāh, 7 11.15]
tatkasya hetoḥ mā tathārūpasya pudgalasya tadātmabhāvasya pramāṇaṃ śrutvā uṣṇaṃ rudhiraṃ mukhādāgacchet maraṇaṃ vā nigacchet maraṇamātrakaṃ vā duḥkham āgāḍhamābādhaṃ spṛśet dahyeta vā śokaśalyo vā asyāviśet mahāprapātaṃ vā prapatet upaśuṣyeta vā mlāyeta vā | [ASāh, 7 11.16]
maiva mahāpratibhayaṃ tasyātmabhāvasya pramāṇamaśrauṣīdyasyeme doṣāḥ saṃvidyante | [ASāh, 7 11.17]
na bhagavānāyuṣmataḥ śāriputrasyāvakāśaṃ karoti iyattasyātmabhāvasya pramāṇaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [ASāh, 7 12.1]
dvitīyakam api tṛtīyakamapyāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat ākhyātu me bhagavāṃstasya pudgalasyātmabhāvasya pramāṇam | [ASāh, 7 12.2]
paścimāyā janatāyā ālokaḥ kṛto bhaviṣyati anena vāṅmanaḥkarmaṇā kṛtena saṃcitenopacitenopacitena evaṃ mahāntaṃ mahānirayeṣvātmabhāvaṃ parigṛhṇīteti | [ASāh, 7 12.3]
bhagavānāha eṣa eva śāriputra paścimāyā janatāyā ālokaḥ kṛto bhaviṣyati yadanena vāṅmanoduścaritena akuśalena karmābhisaṃskāreṇa abhisaṃskṛtena saṃcitenācitenopacitena iyacciraduḥkhaṃ pratyanubhaviṣyatīti | [ASāh, 7 12.4]
yā etasyaiva śāriputra duḥkhasyāprameyatā bahuduḥkhatā vyākhyātā eṣa eva śuklāṃśikasya kulaputrasya kuladuhiturvā saṃvego bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 12.5]
tataḥ sa tebhyo dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyebhyaḥ karmabhyo vinivṛtya puṇyābhisaṃskārameva kuryāt jīvitahetor api saddharmaṃ na pratikṣepsyati mā bhūdasmākam api tādṛśair duḥkhaiḥ samavadhānamiti | [ASāh, 7 12.6]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat susaṃvṛtakāyakarmavākkarmamanaskarmaṇā bhagavan kulaputreṇa vā kuladuhitrā vā bhavitavyam | [ASāh, 7 13.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ yatra hi nāma bhagavan evaṃrūpeṇa vāgdurbhāṣitena iyān mahāpuṇyaskandhaḥ prasūyate | [ASāh, 7 13.2]
katamena punarbhagavan karmaṇā iyān mahāpuṇyaskandhaḥ prasūyate | [ASāh, 7 13.3]
bhagavānāha evaṃrūpeṇa subhūte vāgdurbhāṣitena iyān mahāpuṇyaskandhaḥ prasūyate | [ASāh, 7 13.4]
ihaiva te subhūte mohapuruṣāḥ svākhyāte dharmavinaye pravrajitā bhaviṣyanti ya imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ dūṣayitavyāṃ maṃsyante pratikṣeptavyāṃ maṃsyante pratibādhitavyāṃ maṃsyante | [ASāh, 7 13.5]
prajñāpāramitāyāṃ ca pratibādhitāyāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ buddhabodhiḥ pratibādhitā bhavati | [ASāh, 7 13.6]
buddhabodhau pratibādhitāyām atītānāgatapratyutpannānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ sarvajñatā pratibādhitā bhavati | [ASāh, 7 13.7]
sarvajñatāyāṃ pratibādhitāyāṃ saddharmaḥ pratibādhito bhavati | [ASāh, 7 13.8]
saddharme pratibādhite tathāgataśrāvakasaṃghaḥ pratibādhito bhavati | [ASāh, 7 13.9]
tathāgataśrāvakasaṃghe 'pi pratibādhite evaṃ tasya sarveṇa sarvaṃ sarvathā sarvaṃ triratnātparibāhyabhāvo bhavati aprameyāsaṃkhyeyataraś ca mahānakuśalakarmābhisaṃskāraḥ parigṛhīto bhavati | [ASāh, 7 13.10]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat ko 'tra bhagavan hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yatsa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ pratibādhitavyāṃ maṃsyate bhagavānāha mārādhiṣṭhito vā subhūte sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 14.1]
duṣprajñasaṃvartanīyena vā karmaṇā gambhīreṣu dharmeṣu nāsya śraddhā nāsya prasādaḥ | [ASāh, 7 14.2]
ābhyāṃ subhūte dvābhyāṃ pāpābhyāṃ dharmābhyāṃ samanvāgataḥ sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ pratibādhiṣyate | [ASāh, 7 14.3]
punaraparaṃ subhūte sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā pāpamitrahastagato vā bhaviṣyati anabhiyukto vā bhaviṣyati skandhābhiniviṣṭo vā bhaviṣyati ātmotkarṣī pareṣāṃ paṃsako doṣāntaraprekṣī vā bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 7 14.4]
ebhirapi subhūte caturbhirākāraiḥ sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā samanvāgato bhaviṣyati ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāṃ deśyamānāmupadiśyamānāṃ pratibādhitavyāṃ maṃsyate iti | [ASāh, 7 14.5]
{ASāh, 8}
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat duradhimocā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā anabhiyuktena kuśalamūlavirahitena pāpamitrahastagatena | [ASāh, 8 1.1]
bhagavānāha evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 8 1.2]
duradhimocā subhūte prajñāpāramitā anabhiyuktena parīttakuśalamūlena durmedhasā anarthikena alpaśrutena hīnaprajñena pāpamitropastabdhena aśuśrūṣaṇāparipṛcchakajātīyena kuśaleṣu dharmeṣvanabhiyuktena | [ASāh, 8 1.3]
subhūtirāha kiyadgambhīrā bateyaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitā duradhimocatayā bhagavānāha rūpaṃ subhūte abaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ rūpāsvabhāvatvātsubhūte rūpamabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.2]
evaṃ vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.3]
vijñānaṃ subhūte abaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ vijñānāsvabhāvatvātsubhūte vijñānamabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.5]
rūpasya subhūte pūrvānto 'baddho 'muktaḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.6]
tatkasya hetoḥ pūrvāntāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte rūpam | [ASāh, 8 2.7]
rūpasya subhūte aparānto 'baddho 'muktaḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.8]
tatkasya hetoḥ aparāntāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte rūpam | [ASāh, 8 2.9]
pratyutpannaṃ subhūte rūpam abaddhamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.10]
tatkasya hetoḥ pratyutpannāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte pratyutpannaṃ rūpam | [ASāh, 8 2.11]
evaṃ vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.12]
vijñānasya subhūte pūrvānto 'baddho 'muktaḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.13]
tatkasya hetoḥ pūrvāntāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte vijñānam | [ASāh, 8 2.14]
vijñānasya subhūte aparānto 'baddho 'muktaḥ | [ASāh, 8 2.15]
tatkasya hetoḥ aparāntāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte vijñānam | [ASāh, 8 2.16]
pratyutpannaṃ subhūte vijñānamabaddhamamuktam | [ASāh, 8 2.17]
tatkasya hetoḥ pratyutpannāsvabhāvaṃ hi subhūte pratyutpannaṃ vijñānam | [ASāh, 8 2.18]
subhūtirāha duradhimocā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā paramaduradhimocā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā anabhiyuktena anavaropitakuśalamūlena pāpamitrahastagatena māravaśagatena kusīdena hīnavīryeṇa muṣitasmṛtinā duṣprajñena | [ASāh, 8 3.1]
bhagavānāha evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 8 3.2]
duradhimocā subhūte prajñāpāramitā paramaduradhimocā subhūte prajñāpāramitā anabhiyuktena anavaropitakuśalamūlena pāpamitrahastagatena māravaśagatena kusīdena hīnavīryeṇa muṣitasmṛtinā duṣprajñena | [ASāh, 8 3.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ yā subhūte rūpaviśuddhiḥ sā phalaviśuddhiḥ yā phalaviśuddhiḥ sā rūpaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.4]
iti hi subhūte rūpaviśuddhiś ca phalaviśuddhiś ca advayam etad advaidhīkāram abhinnam achinnam | [ASāh, 8 3.5]
iti hi subhūte phalaviśuddhito rūpaviśuddhī rūpaviśuddhitaḥ phalaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.6]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.7]
yā subhūte vijñānaviśuddhiḥ sā phalaviśuddhiḥ yā phalaviśuddhiḥ sā vijñānaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.8]
iti hi subhūte vijñānaviśuddhiś ca phalaviśuddhiś ca advayametad advaidhīkāram abhinnamacchinnam | [ASāh, 8 3.9]
iti hi subhūte phalaviśuddhito vijñānaviśuddhir vijñānaviśuddhitaḥ phalaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.10]
punaraparaṃ subhūte yā rūpaviśuddhiḥ sā sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ yā sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ sā rūpaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.11]
iti hi subhūte rūpaviśuddhiś ca sarvajñatāviśuddhiś ca advayametad advaidhīkāram abhinnam achinnam | [ASāh, 8 3.12]
iti hi subhūte sarvajñatāviśuddhito rūpaviśuddhiḥ rūpaviśuddhitaḥ sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.13]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.14]
yā subhūte vijñānaviśuddhiḥ sā sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.15]
yā sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ sā vijñānaviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.16]
iti hi subhūte vijñānaviśuddhiś ca sarvajñatāviśuddhiś ca advayametad advaidhīkāram abhinnam achinnam | [ASāh, 8 3.17]
iti hi subhūte sarvajñatāviśuddhito vijñānaviśuddhiḥ vijñānaviśuddhitaḥ sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 3.18]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat gambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.1]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.2]
āha avabhāsakarī bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.3]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.4]
āha āloko bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.5]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.6]
āha apratisaṃdhirbhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.7]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.8]
āha asaṃkleśo bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.9]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.10]
āha aprāptiranabhisamayo bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.11]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.12]
āha anabhinirvṛttir bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.13]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.14]
āha atyantānupapattirbhagavan prajñāpāramitā kāmadhāturūpadhātvārūpyadhātuṣu | [ASāh, 8 4.15]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.16]
āha na jānāti na saṃjānīte bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 4.17]
bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.18]
āha kiṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitā na jānāti na saṃjānīte bhagavānāha rūpaṃ śāriputra prajñāpāramitā na jānāti na saṃjānīte | [ASāh, 8 4.19]
tatkasya hetoḥ viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.20]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 4.21]
vijñānaṃ śāriputra prajñāpāramitā na jānāti na saṃjānīte | [ASāh, 8 4.22]
tatkasya hetoḥ viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.23]
āha prajñāpāramitā bhagavan sarvajñatāyā nāpakāraṃ karoti nopakāraṃ karoti bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.24]
āha prajñāpāramitā bhagavan na kaṃciddharmaṃ parigṛhṇāti na parityajati bhagavānāha viśuddhatvācchāriputra | [ASāh, 8 4.25]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan rūpaviśuddhiḥ bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.26]
āha ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāraviśuddhiḥ | [ASāh, 8 4.27]
ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan vijñānaviśuddhiḥ bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.28]
āha ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan phalaviśuddhiḥ bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.29]
āha ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan sarvajñatāviśuddhiḥ bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.30]
āha ātmaviśuddhito bhagavan na prāptirnābhisamayo bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.31]
āha ātmāparyantatayā bhagavan rūpāparyantatā bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.32]
āha ātmāparyantatayā bhagavan vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānāparyantatā bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.33]
āha ya evamasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya bhagavan avabodhaḥ iyamasya prajñāpāramitā bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.34]
āyuṣmān subhūtirāha sā khalu punariyaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitā nāpare tīre na pare tīre nāpyubhayamantareṇa viprakṛtā sthitā | [ASāh, 8 4.35]
bhagavānāha atyantaviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 4.36]
āyuṣmān subhūtirāha evam api bhagavan saṃjñāsyate bodhisattvo mahāsattvo riñciṣyatīmāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ dūrīkariṣyatīmāṃ prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 8 5.1]
bhagavānāha sādhu sādhu subhūte | [ASāh, 8 5.2]
evam etat subhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 8 5.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ nāmato 'pi hi subhūte saṅgo nimittato 'pi saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.4]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvadiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā svākhyātā sunirdiṣṭā supariniṣṭhitā yatra hi nāma bhagavatā ime 'pi saṅgā ākhyātāḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.5]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat katame te āyuṣman subhūte saṅgāḥ subhūtirāha rūpamāyuṣman śāriputra śūnyamiti saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.6]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.7]
vijñānamāyuṣman śāriputra śūnyamiti saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.8]
atīteṣu dharmeṣvatītā dharmā iti saṃjānīte saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.9]
anāgateṣu dharmeṣvanāgatā dharmā iti saṃjānīte saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.10]
pratyutpanneṣu dharmeṣu pratyutpannā dharmā iti saṃjānīte saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.11]
iyantaṃ puṇyaskandhaṃ prasūyate bodhisattvayānikaḥ pudgalaḥ prathamena cittotpādeneti saṃjānīte saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 5.12]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat katamena ārya subhūte paryāyeṇa saṅgaḥ subhūtirāha sacetkauśika tadbodhicittaṃ saṃjānīte idaṃ tatprathamaṃ bodhicittamiti anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariṇāmayāmīti pariṇāmayati | [ASāh, 8 6.1]
na ca cittaprakṛtiḥ śakyā pariṇāmayituṃ tena kulaputreṇa vā kuladuhitrā vā mahāyānasamprasthitena | [ASāh, 8 6.2]
tasmāttarhi kauśika paraṃ saṃdarśayatā samādāpayatā samuttejayatā saṃpraharṣayatā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau bhūtānugamena saṃdarśayitavyaṃ samādāpayitavyaṃ samuttejayitavyaṃ saṃpraharṣayitavyam | [ASāh, 8 6.3]
evamātmānaṃ ca na kṣiṇoti buddhānujñātayā ca samādāpanayā paraṃ samādāpayati sa kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā | [ASāh, 8 6.4]
imāścāsya sarvāḥ saṅgakoṭyo vivarjitā bhavanti | [ASāh, 8 6.5]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmate subhūtaye sādhukāramadāt sādhu sādhu subhūte yastvaṃ bodhisattvān mahāsattvānimāḥ saṅgakoṭīrbodhayasi | [ASāh, 8 7.1]
tena hi subhūte anyān api sūkṣmatarān saṅgānākhyāsyāmi tān śṛṇu sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuru | [ASāh, 8 7.2]
bhāṣiṣye 'haṃ te | [ASāh, 8 7.3]
sādhu bhagavan ityāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt | [ASāh, 8 7.4]
bhagavānetadavocat iha subhūte śrāddhaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhaṃ nimittato manasi karoti | [ASāh, 8 8.1]
yāvanti khalu punaḥ subhūte nimittāni tāvantaḥ saṅgāḥ | [ASāh, 8 8.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ nimittato hi subhūte saṅgaḥ | [ASāh, 8 8.3]
iti hi so 'tītānāgatapratyutpannānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ ye anāsravā dharmāstānanumode ityanumodya anumodanāsahagataṃ kuśalamūlamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariṇāmayāmīti pariṇāmayati | [ASāh, 8 8.4]
yā khalu punaḥ subhūte dharmāṇāṃ dharmatā na sā atītā vā anāgatā vā pratyutpannā vā | [ASāh, 8 8.5]
yā nātītā nānāgatā na pratyutpannā sā tryadhvanirmuktā | [ASāh, 8 8.6]
yā tryadhvanirmuktā na sā śakyā pariṇāmayituṃ na nimittīkartuṃ nārambaṇīkartum | [ASāh, 8 8.7]
nāpi sā dṛṣṭaśrutamatavijñātā | [ASāh, 8 8.8]
subhūtirāha gambhīrā bhagavan prakṛtirdharmāṇām | [ASāh, 8 9.1]
bhagavānāha viviktatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 9.2]
āha prakṛtigambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 9.3]
bhagavānāha prakṛtiviśuddhatvātsubhūte | [ASāh, 8 9.4]
prakṛtiviviktatvātprakṛtigambhīrā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 9.5]
subhūtirāha prakṛtiviviktā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 9.6]
namaskaromi bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyai | [ASāh, 8 9.7]
bhagavānāha sarvadharmā api subhūte prakṛtiviviktāḥ | [ASāh, 8 10.1]
yā ca subhūte sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiviviktatā sā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 10.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi subhūte akṛtāḥ sarvadharmāstathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhenābhisaṃbuddhāḥ | [ASāh, 8 10.3]
subhūtirāha tasmāttarhi bhagavan sarvadharmā anabhisaṃbuddhās tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena bhagavānāha tathāhi subhūte prakṛtyaiva na te dharmāḥ kiṃcit | [ASāh, 8 10.4]
yā ca prakṛtiḥ sā aprakṛtiḥ yā ca prakṛtiḥ sā prakṛtiḥ sarvadharmāṇāmekalakṣaṇatvādyaduta alakṣaṇatvāt | [ASāh, 8 10.5]
tasmāttarhi subhūte sarvadharmā anabhisaṃbuddhās tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena | [ASāh, 8 10.6]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi subhūte dve dharmaprakṛtī | [ASāh, 8 10.7]
ekaiva hi subhūte sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiḥ | [ASāh, 8 10.8]
yā ca subhūte sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiḥ sā aprakṛtiḥ yā ca aprakṛtiḥ sā prakṛtiḥ | [ASāh, 8 10.9]
evametāḥ subhūte sarvāḥ saṅgakoṭyo vivarjitā bhavanti | [ASāh, 8 10.10]
subhūtirāha gambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.1]
bhagavānāha ākāśagambhīratayā subhūte gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.2]
subhūtirāha duranubodhā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.3]
bhagavānāha tathā hi subhūte na kaścidabhisaṃbudhyate | [ASāh, 8 11.4]
āha acintyā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.5]
bhagavānāha tathā hi subhūte prajñāpāramitā na cittena jñātavyā na cittagamanīyā | [ASāh, 8 11.6]
āha akṛtā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.7]
bhagavānāha kārakānupalabdhitaḥ subhūte akṛtā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 8 11.8]
āha tena hi bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvena prajñāpāramitāyāṃ kathaṃ caritavyam bhagavānāha sacetsubhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caranna rūpe carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.1]
evaṃ sacenna vedanāyāṃ na saṃjñāyāṃ na saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 8 12.2]
sacenna vijñāne carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.3]
sacedrūpamanityamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.4]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 12.5]
sacedvijñānamanityamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.6]
sacedrūpaṃ śūnyamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.7]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 12.8]
sacedvijñānaṃ śūnyamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.9]
sacedrūpam apratipūrṇaṃ pratipūrṇamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.10]
yā ca rūpasyāpratipūrṇatā pratipūrṇatā vā na tadrūpam | [ASāh, 8 12.11]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 12.12]
sacedvijñānam apratipūrṇaṃ pratipūrṇamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.13]
yā ca vijñānasyāpratipūrṇatā pratipūrṇatā vā na tadvijñānam | [ASāh, 8 12.14]
sacedevam api na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 12.15]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvadyadevaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ sasaṅgatā ca asaṅgatā ca khyātāḥ | [ASāh, 8 13.1]
bhagavānāha rūpaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti subhūte na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.2]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 8 13.3]
vijñānaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti subhūte na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.4]
cakṣuḥ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.5]
evaṃ yāvanmanaḥsaṃsparśajā vedanā sasaṅgāsaṅgeti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.6]
pṛthivīdhātuḥ sasaṅgo 'saṅga iti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.7]
yāvadvijñānadhātuḥ sasaṅgo 'saṅga iti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.8]
dānapāramitā sasaṅgāsaṅgeti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.9]
evaṃ śīlapāramitā kṣāntipāramitā vīryapāramitā dhyānapāramitā | [ASāh, 8 13.10]
prajñāpāramitā sasaṅgāsaṅgeti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.11]
evaṃ saptatriṃśadbodhipakṣā dharmā balāni vaiśāradyāni pratisaṃvido 'ṣṭādaśāveṇikā buddhadharmāḥ sasaṅgāsaṅgā iti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.12]
srotaāpattiphalaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.13]
evaṃ sakṛdāgāmiphalamanāgāmiphalamarhattvaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.14]
pratyekabuddhatvaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.15]
buddhatvaṃ sasaṅgamasaṅgamiti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.16]
sarvajñatāpi subhūte sasaṅgāsaṅgeti na carati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 13.17]
evaṃ caran subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na rūpe saṅgaṃ janayati na vedanāyāṃ na saṃjñāyāṃ na saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 8 13.18]
na vijñāne saṅgaṃ janayati | [ASāh, 8 13.19]
na cakṣuṣi saṅgaṃ janayati | [ASāh, 8 13.20]
yāvanna manaḥsaṃsparśajāyāṃ vedanāyāṃ saṅgaṃ janayati | [ASāh, 8 13.21]
na pṛthivīdhātau saṅgaṃ janayati yāvanna vijñānadhātau saṅgaṃ janayati na dānapāramitāyāṃ saṅgaṃ janayati na śīlapāramitāyāṃ na kṣāntipāramitāyāṃ na vīryapāramitāyāṃ na dhyānapāramitāyāṃ na prajñāpāramitāyāṃ saṅgaṃ janayati na bodhipakṣeṣu dharmeṣu na baleṣu na vaiśāradyeṣu na pratisaṃvitsu nāṣṭādaśasvāveṇikeṣu buddhadharmeṣu saṅgaṃ janayati na srotaāpattiphale saṅgaṃ janayati na sakṛdāgāmiphale na anāgāmiphale na arhattve saṅgaṃ janayati na pratyekabuddhatve saṅgaṃ janayati na buddhatve saṅgaṃ janayati nāpi sarvajñatāyāṃ saṅgaṃ janayati | [ASāh, 8 13.22]
tatkasya hetoḥ asaktā abaddhā amuktā asamatikrāntā hi subhūte sarvajñatā | [ASāh, 8 13.23]
evaṃ hi subhūte sarvasaṅgasamatikramāya bodhisattvairmahāsattvaiḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caritavyam | [ASāh, 8 13.24]
subhūtirāha āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvadgambhīro 'yaṃ bhagavan dharmaḥ prajñāpāramitā nāma | [ASāh, 8 14.1]
yā deśyamānāpi na parihīyate adeśyamānāpi na parihīyate | [ASāh, 8 14.2]
deśyamānāpi na vardhate | [ASāh, 8 14.3]
adeśyamānāpi na vardhate | [ASāh, 8 14.4]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat sādhu sādhu subhūte | [ASāh, 8 14.5]
evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 8 14.6]
tadyathāpi nāma subhūte tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddho yāvajjīvaṃ tiṣṭhannākāśasya varṇaṃ bhāṣeta nākāśasya vṛddhirbhavet | [ASāh, 8 14.7]
abhāṣyamāṇe 'pi varṇe naivākāśasya parihānirbhavet | [ASāh, 8 14.8]
tadyathāpi nāma subhūte māyāpuruṣo bhāṣyamāṇe 'pi varṇe nānunīyate na saṃkliśyate abhāṣyamāṇe 'pi varṇe na pratihanyate na saṃkliśyate | [ASāh, 8 14.9]
evameva subhūte yā dharmāṇāṃ dharmatā sā deśyamānāpi tāvatyeva adeśyamānāpi tāvatyeva | [ASāh, 8 14.10]
sthaviraḥ subhūtirāha duṣkarakārako bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo yo gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāvayan na saṃsīdati notplavate | [ASāh, 8 15.1]
atra ca nāma yogamāpadyate na ca pratyudāvartate | [ASāh, 8 15.2]
ākāśabhāvanaiṣā bhagavan yaduta prajñāpāramitābhāvanā | [ASāh, 8 15.3]
namaskartavyāste bhagavan bodhisattvā mahāsattvāḥ yairayaṃ saṃnāhaḥ saṃnaddhaḥ | [ASāh, 8 15.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ ākāśena sārdhaṃ sa bhagavan saṃnaddhukāmo yaḥ sattvānāṃ kṛtaśaḥ saṃnāhaṃ badhnāti | [ASāh, 8 15.5]
mahāsaṃnāhasaṃnaddho bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ | [ASāh, 8 15.6]
śūro bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo ya ākāśasamānāṃ sattvānāṃ dharmadhātusamānāṃ sattvānāṃ kṛtaśaḥ saṃnāhaṃ saṃnaddhukāmo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhukāmaḥ | [ASāh, 8 15.7]
ākāśaṃ sa bhagavan parimocayitukāmaḥ | [ASāh, 8 15.8]
ākāśaṃ sa bhagavan utkṣeptukāmaḥ | [ASāh, 8 15.9]
mahāvīryapāramitāsaṃnāhaprāptaḥ sa bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattvo ya ākāśasamānāṃ dharmadhātusamānāṃ sattvānāṃ kṛtaśaḥ saṃnāhaṃ saṃnahyate | [ASāh, 8 15.10]
atha khalvanyatamo bhikṣuryena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantametadavocat namaskaromi bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyai | [ASāh, 8 16.1]
tathā hi bhagavan prajñāpāramitā na kaṃciddharmamutpādayati na kaṃciddharmaṃ nirodhayati | [ASāh, 8 16.2]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat ya ārya subhūte atra prajñāpāramitāyāmeva yogamāpatsyate kva sa yogamāpatsyate subhūtirāha ākāśe sa kauśika yogamāpatsyate yaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpatsyate | [ASāh, 8 17.1]
abhyavakāśe sa kauśika yogamāpatsyate yaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣitavyaṃ yogamāpattavyaṃ maṃsyate | [ASāh, 8 17.2]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat ājñāpayatu bhagavān | [ASāh, 8 18.1]
tasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ karomi ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ dhārayati | [ASāh, 8 18.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtiḥ śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat samanupaśyasi tvaṃ kauśika taṃ dharmaṃ yasya dharmasya rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ kariṣyasi śakra āha no hīdamārya subhūte | [ASāh, 8 18.3]
subhūtirāha evaṃ kauśika sacedbodhisattvo mahāsattvo yathānirdiṣṭāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthāsyati saiva tasya rakṣāvaraṇaguptirbhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 8 18.4]
atha virahito bhaviṣyati prajñāpāramitayā lapsyante 'sya avatāraprekṣiṇo 'vatāragaveṣiṇo manuṣyāś ca amanuṣyāś ca avatāram | [ASāh, 8 18.5]
api ca kauśika ākāśasya sa rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhātavyāṃ manyeta yo bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhātavyāṃ manyeta prajñāpāramitāyāṃ carataḥ | [ASāh, 8 18.6]
tatkiṃ manyase kauśika pratibalastvaṃ pratiśrutkāyā rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhātum śakra āha na hyetadārya subhūte | [ASāh, 8 18.7]
subhūtirāha evameva kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran viharan pratiśrutkopamāḥ sarvadharmā iti parijānāti | [ASāh, 8 18.8]
sa ca tānna manyate na samanupaśyati na jānāti na saṃjānīte | [ASāh, 8 18.9]
te ca dharmā na vidyante na saṃdṛśyante na saṃvidyante nopalabhyante iti viharati | [ASāh, 8 18.10]
sacedevaṃ viharati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 8 18.11]
atha khalu buddhānubhāvena ye trisāhasramahāsāhasre lokadhātau catvāro mahārājānaḥ sarve ca śakrā devendrāḥ sarve ca mahābrahmāṇaḥ sahāpatiś ca mahābrahmā te sarve yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntāḥ | [ASāh, 8 19.1]
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasābhivandya bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ekānte 'tiṣṭhan | [ASāh, 8 19.2]
ekānte sthitāś ca te mahārājānaḥ sarve ca śakrā devendrāḥ sarve ca brahmakāyikā devā mahābrahmāṇaśca sahāpatiś ca mahābrahmā buddhānubhāvena buddhādhiṣṭhānena buddhasahasraṃ samanvāharanti sma | [ASāh, 8 19.3]
ebhireva nāmabhirebhireva padairebhirevākṣaraiḥ subhūtināmadheyaireva bhikṣubhiriyameva prajñāpāramitopadiṣṭā ayameva prajñāpāramitāparivartaḥ | [ASāh, 8 19.4]
tatrāpi śakrā eva devendrāḥ paripṛcchanti sma paripraśnayanti sma asmin eva pṛthivīpradeśe iyameva prajñāpāramitā bhāṣitā | [ASāh, 8 19.5]
maitreyo 'pi bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya asmin eva pṛthivīpradeśe enāmeva prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣiṣyate iti | [ASāh, 8 19.6]
{ASāh, 9}
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat prajñāpāramiteti bhagavan nāmadheyamātram etat | [ASāh, 9 1.1]
tacca nāma idamiti nopalabhyate | [ASāh, 9 1.2]
vāgvastveva nāmetyucyate | [ASāh, 9 1.3]
sāpi prajñāpāramitā na vidyate nopalabhyate | [ASāh, 9 1.4]
yathaiva nāma tathaiva prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 1.5]
yathā prajñāpāramitā tathā nāma | [ASāh, 9 1.6]
dharmadvayametanna vidyate nopalabhyate | [ASāh, 9 1.7]
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ bhagavan maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo 'nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya ebhireva nāmabhiḥ ebhireva padaiḥ ebhirevākṣaraiḥ asmin eva pṛthivīpradeśe prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣiṣyate evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat tathā hi subhūte maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na rūpaṃ nityaṃ nānityaṃ na rūpaṃ baddhaṃ na muktam atyantaviśuddhamityabhisaṃbhotsyate | [ASāh, 9 1.8]
evaṃ nā vedanāṃ na saṃjñāṃ na saṃskārān | [ASāh, 9 1.9]
na vijñānaṃ nityaṃ nānityam na vijñānaṃ baddhaṃ na muktam atyantaviśuddham ityabhisaṃbhotsyate | [ASāh, 9 1.10]
anena subhūte kāraṇena maitreyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhya ebhireva nāmabhirebhireva padavyañjanairasmin eva pṛthivīpradeśe imāmeva prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣiṣyate | [ASāh, 9 1.11]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat pariśuddhā bateyaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitā bhagavānāha rūpaviśuddhitaḥ subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.1]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 9 2.2]
vijñānaviśuddhitaḥ subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.3]
rūpānutpādānirodhāsaṃkleśāvyavadānaviśuddhitaḥ subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.4]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 9 2.5]
vijñānānutpādānirodhāsaṃkleśāvyavadānaviśuddhitaḥ subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.6]
ākāśaviśuddhitaḥ subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.7]
rūpanirupalepāparigrahatayā subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.8]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 9 2.9]
vijñānanirupalepāparigrahatayā subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.10]
ākāśapratiśrutkāvacanīyapravyāhāranirupalepatayā subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.11]
sarvopalepānulepadharmānupalepatayā subhūte pariśuddhā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 2.12]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat sulabdhā bata lābhāsteṣāṃ bhagavan kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca yeṣāmiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā śrotrāvabhāsamapyāgamiṣyati prāgeva ya udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti | [ASāh, 9 3.1]
na teṣāṃ cakṣūrogo bhaviṣyati na śrotrarogo na ghrāṇarogo na jihvārogo na kāyarogo bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 9 3.2]
na dhandhāyitatā bhaviṣyati na te viṣamāparihāreṇa kālaṃ kariṣyanti | [ASāh, 9 3.3]
bahūni caiṣāṃ devatāsahasrāṇi pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nubaddhāni bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 9 3.4]
aṣṭamīṃ caturdaśīṃ pañcadaśīṃ ca sa dharmabhāṇakaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā yatra yatra prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣiṣyate tatra tatra bahutaraṃ puṇyaṃ prasaviṣyati | [ASāh, 9 3.5]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 9 3.6]
bahūni subhūte tasya kulaputrasya vā kuladuhiturvā devatāsahasrāṇi pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nubaddhāni bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 9 3.7]
bahūni ca devatāsahasrāṇi tatrāgamiṣyanti sarvāṇi dharmaśravaṇārthikāni | [ASāh, 9 3.8]
tāni ca rakṣāvaraṇaguptiṃ saṃvidhāsyanti tasya dharmabhāṇakasya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣamāṇasya | [ASāh, 9 3.9]
tatkasya hetoḥ sadevamānuṣāsurasya hi subhūte lokasya prajñāpāramitā anuttaraṃ ratnam | [ASāh, 9 3.10]
ato 'pi subhūte kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā tatonidānaṃ bahutaraṃ puṇyaṃ prasaviṣyati | [ASāh, 9 3.11]
api tu khalu punaḥ subhūte bahavo 'ntarāyā bhaviṣyanti asyā gambhīrāyāḥ prajñāpāramitāyā likhyamānāyā udgṛhyamāṇāyā dhāryamāṇāyā vācyamānāyāḥ paryavāpyamānāyāḥ pravartyamānāyā upadiśyamānāyā uddiśyamānāyāḥ svādhyāyyamānāyāḥ | [ASāh, 9 3.12]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi subhūte bahupratyarthikāni mahāratnāni bhavanti | [ASāh, 9 3.13]
yathāsāraṃ ca gurutarapratyarthikāni bhavanti | [ASāh, 9 3.14]
anuttaraṃ cedaṃ subhūte mahāratnaṃ lokasya yaduta prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 3.15]
hitāya sukhāya pratipannā lokasya | [ASāh, 9 3.16]
sarvadharmāṇām anutpādāyānirodhāyāsaṃkleśāyāvināśayogena pratyupasthitā | [ASāh, 9 3.17]
na ca subhūte prajñāpāramitā kaṃciddharmamālīyate na kaṃciddharmaṃ saṃkliśyate na kaṃciddharmaṃ parigṛhṇāti | [ASāh, 9 3.18]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi subhūte sarve te dharmā na saṃvidyante nopalabhyante | [ASāh, 9 3.19]
anupalabdhitaḥ subhūte anupaliptā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 3.20]
anupalipteti subhūte iyaṃ prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 3.21]
tathā hi subhūte rūpanirupalepatayā anupalipteyaṃ prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 3.22]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 9 3.23]
vijñānanirupalepatayā subhūte anupalipteyaṃ prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 3.24]
sacedevam api subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na saṃjānīte carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 9 3.25]
sā khalu punariyaṃ subhūte prajñāpāramitā na kasyaciddharmasyāveśikā vā niveśikā vā saṃdarśikā vā nidarśikā vā āvāhikā vā nirvāhikā vā | [ASāh, 9 3.26]
atha khalu saṃbahulāni devaputrasahasrāṇi antarīkṣe kilakilāprakṣveḍitena cailavikṣepānakārṣuḥ dvitīyaṃ batedaṃ dharmacakrapravartanaṃ jambūdvīpe paśyāma iti cāvocan | [ASāh, 9 4.1]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtiṃ sthavirametadavocat nedaṃ subhūte dvitīyaṃ dharmacakrapravartanaṃ nāpi kasyaciddharmasya pravartanaṃ vā nivartanaṃ vā | [ASāh, 9 4.2]
evamiyaṃ subhūte bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 9 4.3]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat mahāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavaṃstasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya yasyāsaṅgatā sarvadharmeṣu yo 'sāvanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhukāmo na ca kaṃciddharmamabhisaṃbudhyate dharmacakraṃ ca pravartayiṣyati na ca kaṃciddharmaṃ saṃdarśayiṣyati | [ASāh, 9 5.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ na hi kaściddharmo ya upalabhyate yo vā dharmaḥ sūcyate | [ASāh, 9 5.2]
nāpi kaściddharmaṃ pravartayiṣyati | [ASāh, 9 5.3]
tatkasya hetoḥ atyantānabhinirvṛttā hi bhagavan sarvadharmāḥ | [ASāh, 9 5.4]
nāpi kaṃciddharmaṃ nivartayiṣyati | [ASāh, 9 5.5]
tatkasya hetoḥ ādyanabhinirvṛttā hi bhagavan sarvadharmāḥ prakṛtiviviktatvātsarvadharmāṇām | [ASāh, 9 5.6]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat evametatsubhūte evam etat | [ASāh, 9 6.1]
na hi subhūte śūnyatā pravartate vā nivartate vā | [ASāh, 9 6.2]
nāpi subhūte animittaṃ pravartate vā nivartate vā | [ASāh, 9 6.3]
nāpi subhūte apraṇihitaṃ pravartate vā nivartate vā | [ASāh, 9 6.4]
yā subhūte evaṃ deśanā iyaṃ sā sarvadharmāṇāṃ deśanā | [ASāh, 9 6.5]
naiva ca kenaciddeśitā nāpi kenacicchrutā nāpi kenacitpratīcchitā nāpi kenacitsākṣātkṛtā nāpi kenacitsākṣātkriyate nāpi kenacit sākṣātkariṣyate | [ASāh, 9 6.6]
nāpyanayā dharmadeśanayā kaścitparinirvṛto nāpi parinirvāsyati nāpi parinirvāti | [ASāh, 9 6.7]
nāpyanayā dharmadeśanayā kaściddakṣiṇīyaḥ kṛtaḥ | [ASāh, 9 6.8]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat asatpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan ākāśasattāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.1]
asamasamatāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.2]
viviktapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan atyantaśūnyatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.3]
anavamṛdyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.4]
apadapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan anāmāśarīratāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.5]
asvabhāvapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan anāgatimagatimupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.6]
avacanapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāvikalpatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.7]
anāmapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan skandhānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.8]
agamanapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāgamanatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.9]
asaṃhāryapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāgrāhyatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.10]
akṣayapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan akṣayadharmayogatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.11]
anutpattipāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānabhinirvṛttitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.12]
akārakapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan kārakānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.13]
ajānakapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāṇāmanātmatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.14]
asaṃkrāntipāramiteyaṃ bhagavan cyutyupapattyanupattitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.15]
avinayapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan pūrvāntāparāntapratyutpannārthānupalabdhitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.16]
svapnapratiśrutkāpratibhāsamarīcimāyāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan anutpādavijñāpanatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.17]
asaṃkleśapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan rāgadveṣamohāsvabhāvatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.18]
avyavadānapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan āśrayānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.19]
anupalepapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan ākāśānupalepatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.20]
aprapañcapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmamananasamatikramatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.21]
amananapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan aniñjanatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.22]
acalitapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan dharmadhātusthititāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.23]
virāgapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāvitathatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.24]
asamutthānapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmanirvikalpatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.25]
śāntapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmanimittānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.26]
nirdoṣapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan guṇapāramitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.27]
niḥkleśapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan parikalpāsattāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.28]
niḥsattvapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan bhūtakoṭitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.29]
apramāṇapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmasamutthānāsamutthānatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.30]
antadvayānanugamapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānabhiniveśanatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.31]
asaṃbhinnapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāsaṃbhedanatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.32]
aparāmṛṣṭapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvaśrāvakapratyekabuddhabhūmyaspṛhaṇatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.33]
avikalpapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan vikalpasamatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.34]
aprameyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan apramāṇadharmatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.35]
asaṅgapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāsaṅgatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.36]
anityapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāsaṃskṛtatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.37]
duḥkhapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan ākāśasamadharmatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.38]
śūnyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.39]
anātmapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānabhiniveśanatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.40]
alakṣaṇapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmānabhinirvṛttitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.41]
sarvaśūnyatāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan anantāparyantatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.42]
smṛtyupasthānādibodhipakṣadharmapāramiteyaṃ bhagavaṃsteṣāmanupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.43]
śūnyatānimittāpraṇihitapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan trivimokṣamukhānupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.44]
aṣṭavimokṣapāramiteyaṃ bhagavaṃsteṣāmanupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.45]
navānupūrvavihārapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan prathamadhyānādīnām anupalabdhitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.46]
catuḥsatyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan duḥkhādīnāmanupalabdhitāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.47]
daśapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan dānādīnām anupalabdhitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.48]
balapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan anavamṛdyatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.49]
vaiśāradyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan atyantānavalīnatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.50]
pratisaṃvitpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvajñatāsaṅgāpratighātitām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.51]
sarvabuddhadharmāveṇikapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan gaṇanāsamatikramatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.52]
tathāgatatathatāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāvitathatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.53]
svayaṃbhūpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan sarvadharmāsvabhāvatām upādāya | [ASāh, 9 7.54]
sarvajñajñānapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yaduta prajñāpāramitā sarvadharmasvabhāvasarvākāraparijñānatām upādāyeti | [ASāh, 9 7.55]
{ASāh, 10}
atha khalu śakrasya devānāmindrasyaitadabhūt pūrvajinakṛtādhikārāste kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca bhaviṣyanti bahubuddhāvaropitakuśalamūlāḥ kalyāṇamitraparigṛhītāśca bhaviṣyanti yeṣāmiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā śrotrāvabhāsamapyāgamiṣyati | [ASāh, 10 1.1]
kaḥ punarvādo ya enāmevaṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti | [ASāh, 10 1.2]
udgṛhya dhārayitvā vācayitvā paryavāpya pravartya deśayitvopadiśyoddiśya svādhyāyya tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 1.3]
na te avaramātrakeṇa kuśalamūlena samanvāgatā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 1.4]
bahubuddhaparyupāsitāste kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 1.5]
paripṛṣṭāḥ paripraśnīkṛtāśca te buddhā bhagavanto bhaviṣyanti kulaputraiḥ kuladuhitṛbhiścaināmeva prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 10 1.6]
śrutā ceyaṃ paurvakāṇāmapi tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmantikāt ya enāṃ prajñāpāramitāmetarhyapi śroṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 1.7]
śrutvā codgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 1.8]
bahubuddhāvaropitakuśalamūlāste kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca veditavyāḥ ya etasyāmeva gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyām uddiśyamānāyāṃ svādhyāyyamānāyāṃ nāvaleṣyante na saṃleṣyante na viṣatsyanti na viṣādamāpatsyante na vipṛṣṭhīkariṣyanti mānasam na bhagnapṛṣṭhīkariṣyanti nottrasiṣyanti na saṃtrasiṣyanti na saṃtrāsamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 1.9]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputraḥ śakrasya devānāmindrasya imamevaṃrūpaṃ cetasaiva cetaḥparivitarkamājñāya bhagavantametadavocat yo bhagavan ihaivaṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyāṃ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā abhiśraddadhadavakalpayannadhimucya prasannacitto bodhāya cittamutpādya enāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyaty upadekṣyaty uddekṣyati svādhyāsyati tathatvāya śikṣiṣyate tathatvāya pratipatsyate tathatvāya yogamāpatsyate yathāvinivartanīyo bodhisattvo mahāsattvastathā sa dhārayitavyaḥ | [ASāh, 10 2.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ gambhīrā bhagavan iyaṃ prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 2.2]
na hi bhagavan parīttakuśalamūlenāparipṛcchakajātīyena aśrutvā buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ saṃmukhībhāvataḥ pūrvam acaritavatā ihaiveyamevaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā adhimoktuṃ śakyā | [ASāh, 10 2.3]
ye punar anadhimucya enām anavabudhyamānāḥ pratikṣeptavyāṃ maṃsyante pūrvāntato'pi bhagavaṃstaiḥ kulaputraiḥ kuladuhitṛbhiśceyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā bhāṣyamāṇā pratikṣiptā | [ASāh, 10 2.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ yathāpi nāma parīttatvātkuśalamūlānām | [ASāh, 10 2.5]
na hi bhagavan acaritavadbhiḥ pūrvāntata iyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā śakyā adhimoktum | [ASāh, 10 2.6]
ye'pi ca pratikṣepsyanti enāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣyamāṇām te'pyevaṃ veditavyāḥ pūrvāntato'pyebhiriyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā bhāṣyamāṇā pratikṣiptā | [ASāh, 10 2.7]
tathā hyeṣāmasyāṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ nāsti śraddhāḥ nāsti kṣāntirnāsti rucirnāsti chando nāsti vīryaṃ nāstyapramādo nāstyadhimuktiḥ na caibhiḥ pūrvaṃ buddhā bhagavanto buddhaśrāvakā vā paripṛṣṭāḥ na ca paripraśnīkṛtā iti | [ASāh, 10 2.8]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat gambhīrā ārya śāriputra prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 3.1]
kimatrāścaryaṃ syādyadasyāṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ pūrvam acaritāvī bodhisattvo mahāsattvo nādhimucyeta atha khalu śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat namaskaromi bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyai | [ASāh, 10 3.2]
sarvajñajñānasya sa bhagavannamaskāraṃ karoti yaḥ prajñāpāramitāyai namaskāraṃ karoti | [ASāh, 10 3.3]
bhagavānāha evameva kauśika evametat | [ASāh, 10 3.4]
sarvajñajñānasya sa kauśika namaskāraṃ karoti yaḥ prajñāpāramitāyai namaskāraṃ karoti | [ASāh, 10 3.5]
tatkasya hetoḥ atonirjātā hi kauśika buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ sarvajñatā | [ASāh, 10 3.6]
sarvajñajñānanirjātā ca punaḥ prajñāpāramitā prabhāvyate | [ASāh, 10 3.7]
evamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caritavyam | [ASāh, 10 3.8]
evamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthātavyam | [ASāh, 10 3.9]
evamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ pratipattavyam | [ASāh, 10 3.10]
evamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpattavyam | [ASāh, 10 3.11]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindro bhagavantametadavocat kathaṃ bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthito bhavati kathaṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpadyate evamukte bhagavān śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat sādhu sādhu kauśika | [ASāh, 10 4.1]
sādhu khalu punastvaṃ kauśika yastvaṃ tathāgatamarhantaṃ samyaksaṃbuddhamenamarthaṃ paripraṣṭavyaṃ paripraśnīkartavyaṃ manyase | [ASāh, 10 4.2]
idamapi te kauśika buddhānubhāvena pratibhānamutpannam | [ASāh, 10 4.3]
iha kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran rūpe na tiṣṭhati rūpamiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 4.4]
yataḥ kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvo rūpe na tiṣṭhati rūpamiti na tiṣṭhati evaṃ rūpe yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 4.5]
evaṃ vedanāyāṃ saṃjñāyāṃ saṃskāreṣu | [ASāh, 10 4.6]
vijñāne na tiṣṭhati vijñānamiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 4.7]
yataḥ kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvo vijñāne na tiṣṭhati vijñānamiti na tiṣṭhati evaṃ vijñāne yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 4.8]
rūpamiti kauśika na yojayati yataḥ kauśika rūpamiti na yojayati evaṃ rūpamiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 4.9]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 10 4.10]
vijñānamiti kauśika na yojayati yataḥ kauśika vijñānamiti na yojayati evaṃ vijñānamiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 4.11]
evaṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sthito bhavati | [ASāh, 10 4.12]
evaṃ yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 4.13]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat gambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 5.1]
duravagāhā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 5.2]
durudgrahā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 5.3]
apramāṇā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 5.4]
bhagavānāha evametacchāriputra evametat | [ASāh, 10 5.5]
rūpaṃ gambhīramiti śāriputra na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 5.6]
yataḥ śāriputra rūpaṃ gambhīramiti na tiṣṭhati evaṃ rūpe yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 5.7]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 10 5.8]
vijñānaṃ śāriputra gambhīramiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 5.9]
yataḥ śāriputra vijñānaṃ gambhīramiti na tiṣṭhati evaṃ vijñāne yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 5.10]
rūpaṃ śāriputra gambhīramiti na yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 5.11]
yataḥ śāriputra rūpaṃ gambhīramiti na yogamāpadyate evaṃ rūpaṃ gambhīramiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 5.12]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 10 5.13]
vijñānaṃ śāriputra gambhīramiti na yogamāpadyate | [ASāh, 10 5.14]
yataḥ śāriputra vijñānaṃ gambhīramiti na yogamāpadyate evaṃ vijñānaṃ gambhīramiti na tiṣṭhati | [ASāh, 10 5.15]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat gambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā avinivartanīyasya vyākṛtasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya purato bhāṣitavyā | [ASāh, 10 6.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ sa hi bhagavan na kāṅkṣiṣyati na vicikitsiṣyati na dhandhāyiṣyati na vivadiṣyati | [ASāh, 10 6.2]
atha khalu śakro devānāmindra āyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat sacetpunarārya śāriputra avyākṛtasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya purata iyaṃ prajñāpāramitā bhāṣyeta ko doṣo bhavet evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputraḥ śakraṃ devānāmindrametadavocat dūrataḥ sa kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattva āgato veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 10 7.1]
cirayānasamprasthitaḥ paripakvakuśalamūlaḥ sa kauśika bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ yo'vyākṛta imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ lapsyate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya | [ASāh, 10 7.2]
śrutvā ca nottrasiṣyati na saṃtrasiṣyati na saṃtrāsamāpatsyate | [ASāh, 10 7.3]
na cedānīmasau cireṇa vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ | [ASāh, 10 7.4]
āsannaṃ tasya vyākaraṇaṃ veditavyam | [ASāh, 10 7.5]
sa bodhisattvo mahāsattvo naikaṃ vā dvau vā trīn vā tathāgatānarhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhānatikramiṣyati tato vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [ASāh, 10 7.6]
api tu tān ārāgayiṣyati ārāgayitvā tāṃstathāgatānarhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddhānna virāgayiṣyati | [ASāh, 10 7.7]
tathāgatadarśanaṃ ca vyākaraṇenāvandhyaṃ kariṣyati tathāgatadarśanācca tato vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [ASāh, 10 7.8]
yāvacca vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau tāvadavandhyaṃ kariṣyati tathāgatadarśanavandanaparyupāsanopasthānaṃ yāvannānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddha iti | [ASāh, 10 7.9]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat dūrataḥ sa bhagavan bodhisattvo mahāsattva āgato bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 10 8.1]
cirayānasamprasthitaḥ | [ASāh, 10 8.2]
paripakvakuśalamūlo hi bhagavan sa bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ ya imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ lapsyate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya | [ASāh, 10 8.3]
kaḥ punarvādo'tra yaḥ śrutvā codgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyatyupadekṣyatyuddekṣyati svādhyāsyati | [ASāh, 10 8.4]
atha khalu bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evametacchāriputra evametat | [ASāh, 10 9.1]
dūrataḥ sa śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattva āgato veditavyaḥ | [ASāh, 10 9.2]
cirayānasamprasthitaḥ | [ASāh, 10 9.3]
paripakvakuśalamūlo hi sa śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhaviṣyati ya imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ lapsyate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya | [ASāh, 10 9.4]
kaḥ punarvādo'tra yaḥ śrutvā codgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyatyupadekṣyatyuddekṣyati svādhyāsyati | [ASāh, 10 9.5]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat pratibhāti me bhagavan pratibhāti me sugata aupamyodāharaṇam | [ASāh, 10 10.1]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan yo'yaṃ bodhisattvayānikaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā svapnāntaragato'pi bodhimaṇḍe niṣīdet veditavyametadbhagavan ayaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattva āsanno'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodher abhisaṃbodhāyeti | [ASāh, 10 10.2]
evameva bhagavan yaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ lapsyate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya kaḥ punarvādaḥ śrutvā codgrahītuṃ dhārayituṃ vācayituṃ paryavāptuṃ pravartayituṃ deśayituṃ upadeṣṭuṃ uddeṣṭuṃ svādhyāpanāya | [ASāh, 10 10.3]
veditavyametadbhagavan dūrato'yaṃ bodhisattvayānikaḥ pudgala āgataścirayānasamprasthitaḥ | [ASāh, 10 10.4]
āsanno'yaṃ bodhisattvayānikaḥ pudgalo vyākaraṇasya | [ASāh, 10 10.5]
vyākariṣyantyenaṃ buddhā bhagavanto bodhisattvaṃ mahāsattvamanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherabhisaṃbodhāyeti | [ASāh, 10 10.6]
cirayānasamprasthitaḥ paripakvakuśalamūlo hi sa bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ yasyeyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā upapatsyate'ntaśaḥ śravaṇāyāpi | [ASāh, 10 10.7]
kaḥ punarvādo'tra bhagavan yaḥ kulaputro vā kuladuhitā vā enāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati deśayiṣyatyupadekṣyatyuddekṣyati svādhyāsyati | [ASāh, 10 10.8]
tatkasya hetoḥ bhūyastvena hi bhagavan dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyaiḥ sattvāḥ karmopacayairavihitāḥ teṣāṃ bhūyastvena asyāṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ cittāni pratikūlāni bhaviṣyanti cittāni parivellayiṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 10.9]
na hyanupacitakuśalamūlāḥ sattvā asyāṃ bhūyastvena bhūtakoṭyāṃ praskandanti prasīdanti | [ASāh, 10 10.10]
upacitakuśalamūlāḥ khalu punaste bhagavan sūpacitakuśalamūlāḥ kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca veditavyāḥ yeṣāmasyāṃ bhūtakoṭyāṃ cittaṃ praskandati prasīdati | [ASāh, 10 10.11]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan puruṣo yojanaśatikādaṭavīkāntārād dviyojanaśatikādvā triyojanaśatikādvā caturyojanaśatikādvā pañcayojanaśatikādvā daśayojanaśatikādvā aṭavīkāntārānniṣkrāmet | [ASāh, 10 10.12]
sa niṣkramya paśyetpūrvanimittāni gopālakān vā paśupālakān vā sīmā vā ārāmasaṃpado vā vanasaṃpado vā tato'nyāpi vā nimittāni yairnimittairgrāmo vā nagaraṃ vā nigamo vā sūcyeta | [ASāh, 10 10.13]
tasya tāni pūrvanimittāni dṛṣṭvaivaṃ bhavati yathemāni pūrvanimittāni dṛśyante tathā āsanno me grāmo vā nagaraṃ vā nigamo vā iti | [ASāh, 10 10.14]
sa āśvāsaprāpto bhavati | [ASāh, 10 10.15]
nāsya bhūyaścoramanasikāro bhavati | [ASāh, 10 10.16]
evameva bhagavan yasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyeyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā upavartate veditavyaṃ tena bhagavan abhyāsanno'smyanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ nacireṇa vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsye'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheriti | [ASāh, 10 10.17]
nāpi tenottrasitavyaṃ na saṃtrasitavyaṃ na bhetavyaṃ śrāvakabhūmervā pratyekabuddhabhūmervā | [ASāh, 10 10.18]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi asyemāni pūrvanimittāni saṃdṛśyante yadutemāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ labhate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya | [ASāh, 10 10.19]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evametacchāriputra evametat | [ASāh, 10 10.20]
pratibhātu te śāriputra punarapyetatsthānam yathāpi nāmaitadbuddhānubhāvena vyāharasi vyāhariṣyasi ca | [ASāh, 10 10.21]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan iha kaścideva puruṣo mahāsamudraṃ draṣṭukāmo bhavet | [ASāh, 10 11.1]
sa gacchenmahāsamudraṃ darśanāya | [ASāh, 10 11.2]
yathā yathā ca sa gacchenmahāsamudraṃ darśanāya tathā tathā sacetpaśyetstambaṃ vā stambanimittaṃ vā parvataṃ vā parvatanimittaṃ vā tenaivaṃ veditavyaṃ dūre tāvadito mahāsamudra iti | [ASāh, 10 11.3]
sacenna bhūyaḥ paśyetstambaṃ vā stambanimittaṃ vā parvataṃ vā parvatanimittaṃ vā tenaivaṃ veditavyam abhyāsanna ito mahāsamudra iti | [ASāh, 10 11.4]
tatkasya hetoḥ anupūrvanimno hi mahāsamudraḥ na mahāsamudrasyābhyantare kaścitstambo vā stambanimittaṃ vā parvato vā parvatanimittaṃ veti | [ASāh, 10 11.5]
kiṃcāpi sa na mahāsamudraṃ sākṣātpaśyati cakṣuṣā atha ca punaḥ sa niṣṭhāṃ gacchati abhyāsanno'smi mahāsamudrasya neto bhūyo dūre mahāsamudra iti | [ASāh, 10 11.6]
evameva bhagavan bodhisattvena mahāsattvenemāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śṛṇvatā veditavyam kiṃcāpyahaṃ taistathāgatairarhadbhiḥ samyaksaṃbuddhairna saṃmukhaṃ vyākṛtaḥ atha ca punarabhyāsanno'smyanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodhervyākaraṇasya | [ASāh, 10 11.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hyenāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ labhate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāyeti | [ASāh, 10 11.8]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan vasante pratyupasthite śīrṇaparṇapalāśeṣu nānāvṛkṣeṣu nānāpallavāḥ prādurbhavanti | [ASāh, 10 11.9]
pallaveṣu prādurbhūteṣvāttamanaskā bhavanti jāmbūdvīpakā manuṣyāḥ tāni pūrvanimittāni vaneṣu dṛṣṭvā nacirādvanapuṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca prādurbhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 11.10]
tatkasya hetos tathā hi imāni pūrvanimittāni stambeṣu dṛśyanta iti | [ASāh, 10 11.11]
evameva bhagavan yadā bodhisattvo mahāsattvo labhate imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya upavartate tasyeyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 11.12]
tadā paripakvakuśalaḥ sa bodhisattvo mahāsattvo veditavyaḥ tenaiva pūrvakeṇa kuśalamūlenopanāmiteyaṃ tasmai gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 11.13]
tatra yā devatāḥ pūrvabuddhadarśinyaḥ tāḥ pramuditā bhavanti prītisaumanasyajātāḥ paurvakāṇāmapi bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāmimānyeva pūrvanimittānyabhūvannanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodhervyākaraṇāya | [ASāh, 10 11.14]
nacireṇa batāyaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvo vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheriti | [ASāh, 10 11.15]
tadyathāpi nāma bhagavan strī gurviṇī gurugarbhā | [ASāh, 10 11.16]
tasyā yadā kāyo veṣṭate adhimātraṃ vā kāyaklamatho jāyate na ca sā caṃkramaṇaśīlā bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.17]
alpāhārā ca bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.18]
alpastyānamiddhā ca bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.19]
alpabhāṣyā ca bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.20]
alpasthāmā ca bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.21]
vedanābahulā ca bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.22]
krandantī ca bahulaṃ viharati | [ASāh, 10 11.23]
na ca saṃvāsaśīlā bhavati | [ASāh, 10 11.24]
paurvakeṇāyoniśo manasikāreṇāsevitena niṣevitena bhāvitena bahulīkṛtena imāmevaṃrūpāṃ kāyena vedanāṃ pratyanubhavāmīti tadā veditavyamidaṃ bhagavan yathāsyāḥ pūrvanimittāni saṃdṛśyante tathā nacireṇa bateyaṃ strī prasoṣyate iti | [ASāh, 10 11.25]
evameva bhagavan yadā bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyeyaṃ gambhīrā prajñāpāramitā upavartate darśanāya vandanāya paryupāsanāya śravaṇāya śṛṇvataścaināṃ ramate cittamasyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyām arthikatayā cotpadyate tadā veditavyamidaṃ bhagavan nacireṇa batāyaṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvo vyākaraṇaṃ pratilapsyate'nuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheriti | [ASāh, 10 11.26]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat sādhu sādhu śāriputra | [ASāh, 10 12.1]
idamapi te śāriputra buddhānubhāvena pratibhāti | [ASāh, 10 12.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvatsuparigṛhītāśca suparīttāśca suparīnditāśca ime bodhisattvā mahāsattvāstathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena | [ASāh, 10 12.3]
bhagavānāha tathā hi te subhūte bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bahujanahitāya pratipannā bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyai mahato janakāyasyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca | [ASāh, 10 12.4]
anukampakā anukampāmupādāya anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃboddhukāmāḥ | [ASāh, 10 12.5]
anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyānuttaraṃ dharmaṃ deśayitukāmāḥ | [ASāh, 10 12.6]
subhūtirāha iha bhagavan bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitāyāṃ carataḥ kathaṃ prajñāpāramitābhāvanā paripūriṃ gacchati bhagavānāha yadi subhūte bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran na rūpasya vṛddhiṃ samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.1]
evaṃ na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 10 13.2]
na vijñānasya vṛddhiṃ samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.3]
na rūpasya parihāṇiṃ samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.4]
evaṃ na vedanāyā na saṃjñāyā na saṃskārāṇām | [ASāh, 10 13.5]
na vijñānasya parihāṇiṃ samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.6]
dharmaṃ na samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.7]
adharmamapi na samanupaśyati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 13.8]
evamasya prajñāpāramitābhāvanā paripūriṃ gacchati | [ASāh, 10 13.9]
subhūtirāha acintyamidaṃ bhagavan deśyate | [ASāh, 10 14.1]
bhagavānāha rūpaṃ hi subhūte acintyam | [ASāh, 10 14.2]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 10 14.3]
vijñānaṃ hi subhūte acintyam | [ASāh, 10 14.4]
rūpamacintyamityapi subhūte na saṃjānīte carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 14.5]
evaṃ vedanāsaṃskārāḥ | [ASāh, 10 14.6]
vijñānamacintyamityapi subhūte na saṃjānīte carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 14.7]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat ko'tra bhagavan adhimokṣayiṣyati evaṃ gambhīrāyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyām bhagavānāha yaḥ śāriputra caritāvī bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhaviṣyati prajñāpāramitāyām so'tra prajñāpāramitāyāmadhimokṣayiṣyati | [ASāh, 10 15.1]
āyuṣmān śāriputra āha kathaṃ bhagavan caritāvī bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bhaviṣyati kathaṃ caritāvīti nāmadheyaṃ labhate bhagavānāha iha śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo balāni na kalpayati vaiśāradyāni na kalpayati buddhadharmānapi na kalpayati sarvajñatāmapi na kalpayati | [ASāh, 10 15.2]
tatkasya hetoḥ balāni hi śāriputra acintyāni vaiśāradyānyapyacintyāni buddhadharmā apyacintyāḥ sarvajñatāpyacintyā sarvadharmā apyacintyāḥ | [ASāh, 10 15.3]
evaṃ caritāvī śāriputra bodhisattvo mahāsattvo na kvaciccarati carati prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 15.4]
evaṃ sa caritāvītyucyate caritāvīti nāmadheyaṃ labhate | [ASāh, 10 15.5]
atha khalu āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat gambhīrā bhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 16.1]
ratnarāśirbhagavan prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 16.2]
śuddharāśirbhagavan prajñāpāramitā ākāśaśuddhatāmupādāya | [ASāh, 10 16.3]
āścaryaṃ bhagavan syādyadenāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇatāṃ dhārayatāṃ vācayatāṃ paryavāpnuvatāṃ pravartayatāṃ deśayatāmupadiśatāmuddiśatāṃ svādhyāyatāṃ likhatāṃ ca kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca bahavo'ntarāyā utpadyeran | [ASāh, 10 16.4]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat evametatsubhūte evametat | [ASāh, 10 16.5]
bahavaḥ subhūte antarāyā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇatāṃ dhārayatāṃ vācayatāṃ paryavāpnuvatāṃ pravartayatāṃ deśayatāmupadiśatāmuddiśatāṃ svādhyāyatāṃ likhatāṃ ca kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 10 16.6]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi subhūte imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇatāṃ dhārayatāṃ vācayatāṃ paryavāpnuvatāṃ pravartayatāṃ deśayatāmupadiśatāmuddiśatāṃ svādhyāyatāṃ likhatāṃ ca kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca māraḥ pāpīyānautsukyamāpatsyate'ntarāyaṃ kartum | [ASāh, 10 16.7]
tatra śīghraṃ likhatā sacenmāsena vā māsadvayena vā māsatrayeṇa vā likhyeta likhitavyaiva bhavet | [ASāh, 10 16.8]
sacetsaṃvatsareṇa tato vāpareṇa likhitā bhavet tathāpi likhitavyaiva khalu punaḥ subhūte bhavati tena kulaputreṇa kuladuhitrā vā iyaṃ prajñāpāramitā | [ASāh, 10 16.9]
tatkasya hetoḥ evaṃ hyetatsubhūte bhavati yanmahāratnānāṃ bahavo'ntarāyā utpadyante | [ASāh, 10 16.10]
evamukte āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat iha bhagavan prajñāpāramitāyām udgṛhyamāṇāyāṃ dhāryamāṇāyāṃ vācyamānāyāṃ paryavāpyamānāyāṃ pravartyamānāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyām uddiśyamānāyāṃ svādhyāyyamānāyāṃ likhyamānāyāṃ ca māraḥ pāpīyān bahuprakāramautsukyamāpatsyate antarāyakarmaṇa udyogaṃ ca kariṣyati | [ASāh, 10 17.1]
bhagavānāha kiṃcāpi subhūte māraḥ pāpīyānudyogamāpatsyate antarāyakarmaṇaḥ asyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyām udgṛhyamāṇāyāṃ dhāryamāṇāyāṃ vācyamānāyāṃ paryavāpyamānāyāṃ pravartyamānāyāṃ deśyamānāyām upadiśyamānāyām uddiśyamānāyāṃ svādhyāyyamānāyāṃ likhyamānāyāṃ ca atha ca punarna prasahiṣyate'cchidrasamādānasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasyāntarāyaṃ kartum | [ASāh, 10 17.2]
atha khalvāyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat yadā bhagavan imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgṛhṇatāṃ dhārayatāṃ vācayatāṃ paryavāpnuvatāṃ pravartayatāṃ deśayatāmupadiśatāmuddiśatāṃ svādhyāyatāṃ likhatāṃ ca kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca māraḥ pāpīyānautsukyamāpatsyate antarāyakaraṇāya tadā kathametarhi bhagavan kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca kasya cānubhāvena bhagavaṃste kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat buddhānāṃ śāriputra bhagavatāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānāmanubhāvena te kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 18.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ eṣā hi śāriputra dharmāṇāṃ dharmatā ye te'prameyeṣvasaṃkhyeyeṣu lokadhātuṣu buddhā bhagavantastiṣṭhanti dhriyante yāpayanti te imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ samanvāhariṣyanti parigrahīṣyanti bhāṣyamāṇāmudgṛhyamāṇāṃ dhāryamāṇāṃ vācyamānāṃ paryavāpyamānāṃ pravartyamānāṃ deśyamānām upadiśyamānām uddiśyamānāṃ svādhyāyyamānāṃ likhyamānāṃ ca | [ASāh, 10 18.2]
ye caināṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraścodgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti ca tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante tāṃśca te buddhā bhagavantaḥ samanvāhariṣyanti parigrahīṣyanti ca | [ASāh, 10 18.3]
na hi śāriputra buddhasamanvāhṛtānāṃ buddhaparigṛhītānāṃ ca kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca śakyamantarāyaṃ kartum | [ASāh, 10 18.4]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat ye'pi te bhagavan bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante sarve te bhagavan buddhānubhāvena buddhādhiṣṭhānena buddhaparigraheṇa ca imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca tathatvāya ca śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante evaṃ ca saṃpādayiṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 19.1]
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evametacchāriputra evametat | [ASāh, 10 20.1]
sarve te śāriputra bodhisattvā mahāsattvā buddhānubhāvena buddhādhiṣṭhānena buddhaparigraheṇa ca imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 20.2]
jñātāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.3]
adhiṣṭhitāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.4]
dṛṣṭāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.5]
vyavalokitāste śāriputra tathāgatena buddhacakṣuṣā | [ASāh, 10 20.6]
ye te bodhisattvā mahāsattvā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca tathatvāya ca śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante śrutvodgṛhya dhārayitvā vācayitvā paryavāpya pravartya deśayitvopadiśyoddiśya svādhyāyya likhitvā tathatvāya śikṣamāṇāstathatvāya pratipadyamānāstathatvāya yogamāpadyamānā āsannībhaviṣyantyanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodheḥ tathatvāya sthāsyantyanuttarāyai samyaksaṃbodhaye | [ASāh, 10 20.7]
ye'pi śāriputra enāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ likhitvā dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti na ca tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante na ca tathatvāya pratipatsyante na ca tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante te na tathatvāya śikṣamāṇā na tathatvāya pratipadyamānā na tathatvāya yogamāpadyamānā na tathatāyāṃ sthāsyantyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau te'pi śāriputra tathāgatena jñātāḥ | [ASāh, 10 20.8]
te'pi tathāgatenādhiṣṭhitāḥ | [ASāh, 10 20.9]
te'pi tathāgatena dṛṣṭāḥ | [ASāh, 10 20.10]
te'pi tathāgatena vyavalokitā buddhacakṣuṣā | [ASāh, 10 20.11]
teṣāmapi śāriputra mahārthiko mahānuśaṃso mahāphalo mahāvipākaśca sa pariśramaḥ parispandaśca bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 10 20.12]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi prajñāpāramitā paramārthopasaṃhitā sarvadharmāṇāṃ yathābhūtaprativedhāya pratyupasthitā sarvasattvānām | [ASāh, 10 20.13]
ime khalu punaḥ śāriputra ṣaṭpāramitāpratisaṃyuktāḥ sūtrāntāstathāgatasyātyayena dakṣiṇāpathe pracariṣyanti dakṣiṇāpathātpunareva vartanyāṃ pracariṣyanti vartanyāḥ punaruttarapathe pracariṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 20.14]
navamaṇḍaprāpte dharmavinaye saddharmasyāntardhānakālasamaye samanvāhṛtāste śāriputra tathāgatena kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca | [ASāh, 10 20.15]
tasmin kāle ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti antaśo likhitvā pustakagatāmapi kṛtvā dhārayiṣyanti jñātāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.16]
adhiṣṭhitāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.17]
dṛṣṭāste śāriputra tathāgatena | [ASāh, 10 20.18]
vyavalokitāste śāriputra tathāgatena buddhacakṣuṣā | [ASāh, 10 20.19]
śāriputra āha iyamapi bhagavan prajñāpāramitā evaṃ gambhīrā paścime kāle paścime samaye vaistārikī bhaviṣyatyuttarasyāṃ diśi uttare digbhāge bhagavānāha ye tatra śāriputra uttarasyāṃ diśyuttare digbhāge imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śrutvā atra prajñāpāramitāyāṃ yogamāpatsyante te vaistārikīṃ kariṣyati | [ASāh, 10 21.1]
cirayānasamprasthitāste śāriputra bodhisattvā mahāsattvā veditavyāḥ ya imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti likhiṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyantyupadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante | [ASāh, 10 21.2]
śāriputra āha kiyantaste bhagavan bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaviṣyanti uttarasyāṃ diśi uttare digbhāge bahava utāho alpakāḥ ya imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti likhiṣyanti udgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyanti upadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante bhagavānāha bahavaste śāriputra subahavaḥ uttarāpathe uttarasyāṃ diśyuttare digbhāge bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 22.1]
kiṃcāpi śāriputra bahavaste tebhyo'pi bahubhyo'lpakāste bodhisattvā mahāsattvā bhaviṣyanti ya imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ śroṣyanti likhiṣyantyudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyanti upadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti tathatvāya śikṣiṣyante tathatvāya pratipatsyante tathatvāya yogamāpatsyante prajñāpāramitāyāṃ ca bhāṣyamāṇāyāṃ nāvaleṣyante na saṃleṣyante na viṣatsyanti na viṣādamāpatsyante na vipṛṣṭhīkariṣyanti mānasam na bhagnapṛṣṭhīkariṣyanti nottrasiṣyanti na saṃtrasiṣyanti na saṃtrāsamāpatsyante cirayānasamprasthitāste bodhisattvā mahāsattvā veditavyāḥ | [ASāh, 10 22.2]
anubaddhāstaiḥ paurvakāstathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ paripṛṣṭāḥ paripṛcchitāḥ paripraśnīkṛtāḥ | [ASāh, 10 22.3]
pūjitāśca taiḥ paurvakāstathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ kulaputraiḥ kuladuhitṛbhiśca bodhisattvayānikaiḥ pudgalaiḥ | [ASāh, 10 22.4]
śīleṣu ca te paripūrṇakāriṇo bhaviṣyanti bahujanasya ca te'rthaṃ kariṣyanti yaduta imāmevānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya | [ASāh, 10 22.5]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi teṣāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca mayaiva sarvajñatāpratisaṃyuktaiva kathā kṛtā | [ASāh, 10 22.6]
teṣāṃ jātivyativṛttānāmapi eta eva sarvajñatāpratisaṃyuktāḥ prajñāpāramitāpratisaṃyuktāḥ samudācārā bhaviṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 22.7]
enāmeva ca te kathāṃ kariṣyanti enāmeva ca kathāmabhinandiṣyanti yaduta anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimārabhya | [ASāh, 10 22.8]
teṣu ca susthitāḥ samāhitāśca bhaviṣyanti asyāṃ prajñāpāramitāyām | [ASāh, 10 22.9]
māreṇāpi te na śakyā bhedayitum kutaḥ punaranyaiḥ sattvaiḥ yaduta chandato vā mantrato vā | [ASāh, 10 22.10]
tatkasya hetoḥ yathāpi nāma taddṛḍhasthāmatvādanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [ASāh, 10 22.11]
te ca kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca śrutvā enāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudāraṃ prītiprāmodyaprasādaṃ pratilapsyante | [ASāh, 10 22.12]
bahujanasya ca te kuśalamūlānyavaropayiṣyanti yadutānuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau | [ASāh, 10 22.13]
tatkasya hetoḥ evaṃ hi taiḥ kulaputraiḥ kuladuhitṛbhiśca mamāntike saṃmukhaṃ vāgbhāṣitā bahūni prāṇiśatāni bahūni prāṇisahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatāni bahūni prāṇikoṭīsahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi bodhisattvacaryāṃ caranto vayamanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau prasthāpayiṣyāmaḥ saṃdarśayiṣyāmaḥ samādāpayiṣyāmaḥ samuttejayiṣyāmaḥ saṃpraharṣayiṣyāmaḥ saṃprabhāvayiṣyāmaḥ saṃbodhaye pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyāma iti avinivartanīyān kariṣyāma iti | [ASāh, 10 22.14]
tatkasya hetoḥ anumoditaṃ hi śāriputra mayā teṣāṃ bodhisattvayānikānāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca cittena cittaṃ vyavalokya yairiyaṃ vāgbhāṣitā bodhāya caranto vayaṃ bahūni prāṇiśatāni bahūni prāṇisahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatāni bahūni prāṇikoṭīsahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau prasthāpayiṣyāmaḥ saṃdarśayiṣyāmaḥ samādāpayiṣyāmaḥ samuttejayiṣyāmaḥ saṃpraharṣayiṣyāmaḥ saṃprabhāvayiṣyāmaḥ saṃbodhaye pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyāma iti avinivartanīyān kariṣyāma iti | [ASāh, 10 22.15]
evaṃ ca te kulaputrāḥ kuladuhitaraśca udārādhimuktikā bhaviṣyanti yadanyānyapi te buddhakṣetrāṇyadhyālambitavyāni maṃsyante | [ASāh, 10 22.16]
yatra saṃmukhībhūtāstathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā dharmaṃ deśayiṣyanti tatra saṃmukhībhūtānāṃ tathāgatānāmarhatāṃ samyaksaṃbuddhānām antikātpunarevaināṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ vistareṇa śroṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 22.17]
teṣvapi te buddhakṣetreṣu bahūni prāṇiśatāni bahūni prāṇisahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇiśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatāni bahūni prāṇikoṭīsahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīśatasahasrāṇi bahūni prāṇikoṭīniyutaśatasahasrāṇi anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau prasthāpayiṣyanti saṃdarśayiṣyanti samādāpayiṣyanti samuttejayiṣyanti saṃpraharṣayiṣyanti saṃprabhāvayiṣyanti saṃbodhaye pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyanti avinivartanīyān kariṣyanti | [ASāh, 10 22.18]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat āścaryaṃ bhagavan yāvadidaṃ tathāgatenārhatā samyaksaṃbuddhena atītānāgatapratyutpanneṣu dharmeṣu nāsti kiṃcidadṛṣṭaṃ vā aśrutaṃ vā aviditaṃ vā avijñātaṃ vā | [ASāh, 10 23.1]
na sa kaściddharmo yo na jñāto na sā kāciccaryā sattvānāṃ yā na vijñātā yatra hi nāma anāgatānāmapi bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ caryā jñātā bodhicchandikānām adhyāśayasampannānām ārabdhavīryāṇām | [ASāh, 10 23.2]
ye tasmin kāle imāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitāmudgrahīṣyanti dhārayiṣyanti vācayiṣyanti paryavāpsyanti pravartayiṣyanti deśayiṣyanti upadekṣyantyuddekṣyanti svādhyāsyanti likhiṣyanti ca ye ca tasmin kāle āsāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ pāramitānāṃ kṛtaśaḥ sarvasattvānāmarthāya udyogamāpadya anveṣiṣyante paryeṣiṣyante gaveṣiṣyante teṣāṃ ca kulaputrānāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca anveṣamāṇānāṃ paryeṣamāṇānāṃ kecidgaveṣamāṇā bodhisattvā lapsyante kecinna lapsyante kecid agaveṣayanto 'pi lapsyante enāṃ gambhīrāṃ prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 10 23.3]
kimatra bhagavan kāraṇam evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ śāriputrametadavocat evametacchāriputra evametat | [ASāh, 10 23.4]
nāsti kiṃcittathāgatasya atītānāgatapratyutpanneṣu dharmeṣvadṛṣṭaṃ vā aśrutaṃ vā aviditaṃ vā avijñātaṃ vā | [ASāh, 10 23.5]
tasmin khalu punaḥ śāriputra kāle tasmin samaye kecidbodhisattvā mārgayamāṇāḥ paryeṣamāṇā gaveṣamāṇā api lapsyante imāṃ prajñāpāramitām | [ASāh, 10 23.6]
kecidbodhisattvā amārgayamāṇā aparyeṣamāṇā agaveṣayanto 'pi lapsyante | [ASāh, 10 23.7]
tatkasya hetoḥ tathā hi tairbodhisattvairmahāsattvairiyaṃ prajñāpāramitā pūrvāntato'pi anikṣiptadhurair mārgitā ca paryanviṣṭā ca | [ASāh, 10 23.8]
te tenaiva pūrvakeṇa kuśalamūlacchandena enāṃ prajñāpāramitām amārgayanto'pi aparyeṣamāṇā api agaveṣayanto'pi lapsyante | [ASāh, 10 23.9]
yānyapi ca tato'nyānyapi sūtrāṇi enāmeva prajñāpāramitāmabhivadanti tāni caiṣāṃ svayamevopagamiṣyanti upapatsyante upanaṃsyante ca | [ASāh, 10 23.10]
tatkasya hetoḥ evametacchāriputra bhavati ya enāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bodhisattvo mahāsattvo'nikṣiptadhuro mārgayati ca paryeṣate ca sa jātivyativṛtto'pi janmāntaravyativṛtto'pi enāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ lapsyate | [ASāh, 10 23.11]
tato'nyāni ca sūtrāṇi prajñāpāramitāpratisaṃyuktāni tasya svayamevopagamiṣyanti upapatsyante upanaṃsyante ceti | [ASāh, 10 23.12]
evamukte āyuṣmān śāriputro bhagavantametadavocat ime eva kevalaṃ bhagavaṃsteṣāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca ṣaṭpāramitāpratisaṃyuktāḥ sūtrāntā upapatsyante upanaṃsyante nānye bhagavānāha ye cānye'pi śāriputra gambhīrā gambhīrāḥ sūtrāntā bhaviṣyanti te'pi teṣāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca svayamevopapatsyante svayamevopanaṃsyante ca | [ASāh, 10 24.1]
tatkasya hetoḥ evaṃ hyetacchāriputra bhavati ye bodhisattvā mahāsattvā anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau prasthāpayiṣyanti saṃdarśayiṣyanti samādāpayiṣyanti samuttejayiṣyanti saṃpraharṣayiṣyanti prabhāvayiṣyanti saṃbodhaye pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyanti avinivartanīyān kariṣyanti svayaṃ ca tatra śikṣiṣyante teṣāṃ śāriputra jātivyativṛttānāmapi ime gambhīrā gambhīrā anupalambhapratisaṃyuktāḥ śūnyatāpratisaṃyuktāḥ ṣaṭpāramitāpratisaṃyuktāśca sūtrāntāḥ svayamevopagamiṣyanti svayamevopapatsyante svayamevopanaṃsyante ceti | [ASāh, 10 24.2]
{ASāh, 11}
atha khalu āyuṣmān subhūtirbhagavantametadavocat guṇā ime bhagavaṃsteṣāṃ kulaputrāṇāṃ kuladuhitṝṇāṃ ca bhagavatā parikīrtitāḥ | [ASāh, 11 1.1]
kecitpunarbhagavaṃsteṣāmantarāyā utpatsyante evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantaṃ subhūtimetadavocat bahūni subhūte teṣāṃ mārakarmāṇyantarāyakarāṇy utpatsyante | [ASāh, 11 1.2]
subhūtirāha kiyadrūpāṇi bhagavaṃsteṣāṃ bahūni mārakarmāṇy antarāyakarāṇyutpatsyante bhagavānāha teṣāṃ subhūte bodhisattvānāṃ mahāsattvānāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ bhāṣamāṇānāṃ cireṇa pratibhānamutpatsyate | [ASāh, 11 1.3]
idaṃ subhūte prathamaṃ mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.4]
tad api ca pratibhānaṃ jāyamānameva vikṣepsyate | [ASāh, 11 1.5]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.6]
te vijṛmbhamāṇā hasanta uccagghayanto likhiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.7]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.8]
vikṣiptacittāḥ paryavāpsyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.9]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.10]
anyonyavijñānasamaṅgino likhiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.11]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.12]
smṛtiṃ na pratilapsyante | [ASāh, 11 1.13]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.14]
parasparamupahasanto likhiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.15]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.16]
parasparamuccagghayamānā likhiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.17]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.18]
vikṣiptacakṣuṣo likhiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.19]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.20]
likhatāmanyonyaṃ visāmagrī bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 11 1.21]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.22]
na vayamatra gādhaṃ nāsvādaṃ labhāmahe ityutthāyāsanāt prakramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.23]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.24]
na vayamatra vyākṛtāḥ prajñāpāramitāyām ityaprasannacittā utthāyāsanāt prakramiṣyanti | [ASāh, 11 1.25]
idam api subhūte mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.26]
na no 'tra grāmasya vā nagarasya vā nigamasya vā nāmadheyaṃ parigṛhītaṃ yatra no janma na no 'tra nāma gotraṃ vā gṛhītam na mātāpitrornāma gotraṃ vā gṛhītam nāpi kulasya yatra no janmeti te prajñāpāramitāṃ na śrotavyāṃ maṃsyante tato 'pakramitavyaṃ maṃsyante | [ASāh, 11 1.27]
yathā yathā ca apakramiṣyanti tairyāvadbhiścittotpādaistathā tathā tāvataḥ kalpān saṃsārasya punaḥ punaḥ parigrahīṣyanti yatra taiḥ punareva yogamāpattavyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [ASāh, 11 1.28]
tatkasmāt imāṃ hi subhūte prajñāpāramitāmaśṛṇvanto bodhisattvā mahāsattvā laukikalokottareṣu dharmeṣu na nirjāyante | [ASāh, 11 1.29]
idam api subhūte teṣāṃ mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.30]
punaraparaṃ subhūte bodhisattvayānikāḥ pudgalā imāṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ sarvajñajñānasyāhārikāṃ vivarjya utsṛjya ye te sūtrāntā naiva sarvajñajñānasyāhārikāstān paryeṣitavyān maṃsyante | [ASāh, 11 1.31]
idam api subhūte teṣāṃ mārakarma veditavyam | [ASāh, 11 1.32]
yathā khalu punaḥ subhūte na laukikalokottareṣu śikṣitukāmā na laukikalokottareṣu dharmeṣu niryātukāmā iha prajñāpāramitāyāṃ na śikṣante | [ASāh, 11 1.33]
prajñāpāramitāyām aśikṣamāṇā na laukikalokottareṣu dharmeṣu niryānti | [ASāh, 11 1.34]
evaṃ te parīttabuddhayo laukikalokottarāṇāṃ yathābhūtaparijñāyā mūlaṃ prajñāpāramitāṃ vivarjya utsṛjya praśākhāmadhyālambitavyāṃ maṃsyante | [ASāh, 11 1.35]
